  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a831852c-113e-4cc2-9ea5-2bd768ec0ff4'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText1468519523864012645" style="display:none">One night changed my life forever.<br /><br />Beau Bennett has been my best friend since I can remember. He was my first crush before everything came crashing down, and now he wants more, but it's more than I can give him. Things are different now. I wish I could tell him why, but I can't. <br /><br />I haven’t told anyone.<br /><br />I never knew how much I really needed him until the day he left for college, and I was completely alone.<br /><br />Then one day, Asher Hunt rides into town with his dark, captivating eyes and cocky grin. He doesn't care who I used to be, he's simply breathing life into what’s left. People warn me to stay away from him, but he helps me forget the pain that has held me hostage for so long; something I thought was impossible before he walked into my life.<br /><br />I’ve been hurt. <br /><br />I’ve been saved. <br /><br />And I’ve found hope. <br /><br />I thought my story was written that night, but now I know it was only a new beginning. Until one secret turns my world upside down…<br /><br />Again.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer641030948" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15386606305070283354"><b>5 Amazing Stars!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/d717cd02-7c9e-440a-b8b8-0642f26f5896_zpsaf74fc2f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848760.jpg' alt=' photo d717cd02-7c9e-440a-b8b8-0642f26f5896_zpsaf74fc2f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>When it Rains</i> is one of the most emotional, beautiful and heartbreaking books I have ever read. It captivated me from the very first page and I couldn’t put it down. This book moved me. I ugly cried big time while reading, but it was worth every tear. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I’m lost. I really have no idea where my life goes from here. I want to say it can’t get any worse, but I’ve thought that before and there always seems to be a hole to sing into. Some days I don’t even know if I can go</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText15386606305070283354" style="display:none"><b>5 Amazing Stars!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/d717cd02-7c9e-440a-b8b8-0642f26f5896_zpsaf74fc2f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848760.jpg" alt=" photo d717cd02-7c9e-440a-b8b8-0642f26f5896_zpsaf74fc2f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>When it Rains</i> is one of the most emotional, beautiful and heartbreaking books I have ever read. It captivated me from the very first page and I couldn’t put it down. This book moved me. I ugly cried big time while reading, but it was worth every tear. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I’m lost. I really have no idea where my life goes from here. I want to say it can’t get any worse, but I’ve thought that before and there always seems to be a hole to sing into. Some days I don’t even know if I can go on.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> Meet Kate. Kate is a nineteen year old girl who had something terrible happen to her two years ago. Something that changed her, changed everything. That night, the old Kate died. Someone new has taken her place. Someone lost, sad, lonely. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/88f82bf5-ccb7-4836-8e28-5ae63cff4753_zpsd6298bb4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848761.jpg" alt=" photo 88f82bf5-ccb7-4836-8e28-5ae63cff4753_zpsd6298bb4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kate lives with her mother, and across the street from her best friend, Beau. Beau is the sweetest guy ever.<br><i>
  <blockquote>He’s the one person in the world I trust not to hurt me.</blockquote>
</i><br> He and Kate have known each other since they were five. No matter how withdrawn and distant Kate gets, Beau won’t give up on her. He knows something happened to Kate, she just can’t tell him. She can’t tell anyone. Beau wants to know, to help her. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Something changed you, and I’m going to keep digging until I find out what that is.”</blockquote>
</i> Beau makes things tolerable. But now, he’s leaving for college. He wants Kate to come too, but she can’t. Beau has always had feelings for Kate. At one point in Kate’s life, she would have loved to hear this, but now she just can’t deal. She thinks maybe it’s best if they have a little space, Beau needs to move on with his life, have a normal college experience, not be stuck on someone as damaged as her. <br><br>Kate gets up each morning, works in the diner, comes home, reads/watches tv, then goes to sleep. She repeats this everyday. That is, until someone new comes into town. His name is Asher Hunt. From the first time Kate sees Asher in the diner, she knows there is just something about him. Asher starts coming in and sitting in Kate’s section. He wants to know this beautifully broken girl, he wants to spend time with her. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“I want to know you. I want to know what it is that made you cry, but more than that, I want to know what I have to do to make you happy again.”</blockquote>
</i> Things are different with Asher. He doesn’t expect Kate to act a certain way, he didn’t know her before. He just wants to get her to do new things, spend time with her, get her to open up. Asher is the most beautiful soul. You will fall in love with this guy! Asher also has a broken side. He hides it better than Kate, but it’s there. For the first time, Kate wants to try. <br><b>
  <blockquote>When I’m with Asher, I want to try.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/0c20d412-ee48-4273-bf77-8b2de35d88af_zps5e8d0cc7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848762.jpg" alt=" photo 0c20d412-ee48-4273-bf77-8b2de35d88af_zps5e8d0cc7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>When I look into his stormy blue eyes, I see desire, need and pain. He’s letting me see things that he isn’t showing others. I want to help him with whatever he’s hiding. I think maybe we can help each other.</blockquote>
</b> Eventually, Asher does get Kate to open up. Something she has never been able to do with anyone. Not her mom or her best friend. Asher can bring it out of her. And it feels good to finally let it out. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why did you decide to tell me your secret?” I ask, entwining my fingers with his. “Because I knew it was the only way I’d get you to tell me yours.”</blockquote>
</i><br>The more time Kate and Asher spend together, the closer they become in all ways. Asher is helping Kate. Healing her. Replacing all her bad memories with good. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/f2eff1b3-55a3-45bd-ae74-16635efb079f_zps85717006.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848763.jpg" alt=" photo f2eff1b3-55a3-45bd-ae74-16635efb079f_zps85717006.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>It’s loving, passionate, and intense... it’s everything a kiss should be.<br>It’s everything Asher is.</blockquote>
</b><br>Then there is Beau. Beau finds out about Kate and Asher. Naturally, he’s hurt. He still loves Kate. He still wants to be there for her, but its hard. Although both Beau and Asher play prominent roles in this story, there is no cheating, no love triangle, nothing like that. <br><br>As close as Kate and Asher get, there is still something between them. A secret Asher hasn’t been able to tell Kate...<br><b>
  <blockquote>They say everything happens for a reason. I don’t see any reason for this.</blockquote>
</b> As much as I loved this book, I haven’t been this devastated while reading in quite sometime. This will go in my top 10 all time favorite tearjerkers. I swear it felt like I cried (more like sobbed) for an hour straight while reading. I don’t want to divulge any more that that, but be prepared for tears.<br> Some of my favorite quotes... <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>
    <i>“You don’t live because of me. You live because you let me love you. You made the choice to breathe all on your own…I just helped you find the strength to inhale.” <br><br>“I’ll never regret you. You’re everything to me.”<br><br>“You gave me my life back. You cared about me enough to push back my demons. You made me want to be with you every minute of the day because you made me feel things that no one else could. And whether you’re lying beside me or living in my memories, I will love you. Forever. Always.”<br><br>“All the stars shine for you, Asher.” </i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/e311f58e-9f85-4ef0-8a58-b4ff10e534c0_zps42402c3f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848764.jpg" alt=" photo e311f58e-9f85-4ef0-8a58-b4ff10e534c0_zps42402c3f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>The best chapter of my life...</b> <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ba961fbd-69e1-407d-93d6-adb86355f85b_zps43d4e2a2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848765.jpg" alt=" photo ba961fbd-69e1-407d-93d6-adb86355f85b_zps43d4e2a2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>There’s a difference between <u>soul mates</u> and <u>true love.</u> Looking at the surface, they are similar, but when I dug deep down inside, I found they were different. Is one type of love better than the other? I don’t know but I’m lucky enough to have found them both.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><i>When it Rains</i> has it all. It’s beautifully written, the story just flows. The characters are lovable. Even though I feel like my heart was torn from my chest, I can’t think of one thing I didn’t love about this book. Not one. It was the perfect read for me. Moving, heartbreaking, exceptionally good. It is also a stand alone with a hea. This will go towards the top of my favorite reads for 2013.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/c9a01d1f-7ad7-4366-9cd8-8e980ef45e66_zps91554e7e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380425331i/848766.jpg" alt=" photo c9a01d1f-7ad7-4366-9cd8-8e980ef45e66_zps91554e7e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><i>**ARC kindly provided by author in exchange for an honest review**</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_721663120" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/721663120" />
    <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites"><img alt="Alexis *Reality Bites*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1404308282p2/5587514.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/721663120?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5587514-alexis-reality-bites?shelf=secrets">secrets</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer721663120" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10894938497073014916">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br/>4.5STARS out of 5<br/>Genre:New Adult Romance<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436928i/883404.jpg' alt=' photo 60ffb851-4327-4469-ad0e-0235f1279210_zpsaab0a313.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Words cannot express.. <b>I LOVED THIS BOOK!</b> When it Rains is a book you read slowly while you savor the words written on each page. This was not an easy read I spent the majority of it in tears. So readers be sure to keep the Kleenex near.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>‘I squeezed my eyes shut, feeling like I was drowning with no way to get to the surface. I’ve never felt such intense physical and emotional pain all at on</b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText10894938497073014916" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4.5STARS out of 5<br>Genre:New Adult Romance<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436928i/883404.jpg" alt=" photo 60ffb851-4327-4469-ad0e-0235f1279210_zpsaab0a313.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Words cannot express.. <b>I LOVED THIS BOOK!</b> When it Rains is a book you read slowly while you savor the words written on each page. This was not an easy read I spent the majority of it in tears. So readers be sure to keep the Kleenex near.<br><br><i>
  <b>‘I squeezed my eyes shut, feeling like I was drowning with no way to get to the surface. I’ve never felt such intense physical and emotional pain all at once. It was the absolute worst moment of my life. <br>It still is.’</b>
</i> -Kate<br><br><b>Forever Changed</b><br>When the book opens we meet Kate a young track star with dreams to go to college and one day become a lawyer. One night turns her world upside down shattering those dreams changing the course her life takes. Kate becomes a shell of her former self, she quits track and cuts herself off from friends. Her best friend Beau sticks by her though he has no idea why she has changed from the outgoing girl he<b> once</b> knew.<br><br>Beau and Kate have been friends since child hood. She remembers clearly the day she stopped seeing him as a friend and began to look at him as a guy she wants to be<b> more</b> than friends with. It was in middle school. This is not a feeling Beau returns towards Kate because he is too busy hooking up with other girls throughout high school.<br><br><i>
  <b>‘I was the princess waiting for my prince to come save me from the top of the highest tower. <br>Now, I’m unreachable . . . even for Beau.’</b>
</i> -Kate<br><br>When the time grows close for Beau to leave for college he confesses his feelings to Kate; letting her know he wants to be more than just friends. Kate voices that she is not ready; so he tells her that he’ll wait.<br><br>Kate spends her days working at the diner, the same one her mother works at. It is there that she meets<b> him</b>..One day<b> he</b> enters and<b> they</b> lock eyes. <br><br><b>I can’t take it anymore.<i> “Do I know you?” </i>I ask. </b><br><b><i>“Only if you count the little staring contest we had yesterday,”</i> he replies, letting the corners of his mouth turn up a little more.<i> “My name’s Asher Hunt.”</i></b><br><br>Asher befriends Kate and brings her back to <b>life</b>. Asher challenges her in ways no one else has as he bravely pulls her out of the shell she has been living in. The pages with him and her..one on one held some of my favorite moments, him getting her to open<b> up</b> and <b>live</b> life in a way no one else could.<i> SWOON WORTHY MOMENTS</i>!<br><br><b>
  <i>'Asher tries to understand me layer by layer while Beau goes straight for the center.'</i>
</b> -Kate<br><br>When Beau learns that Kate has been seeing Asher on more then just a platonic level he is none to pleased. And neither is her mother for that matter because Asher has a bit of a bad boy reputation in the small town of Carrington.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380410620i/805376.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mhwho7a0M11rx0x5qo1_500_zps2459fab5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>SECRETS</b><br>Both Asher and Kate are holding in painful secrets and they connect on this level and it grows from there. The author does not hold the secrets in long; she allows the characters to reveal them in a timely manner that will not turn readers off. <b>
  <u>THAT </u>
</b>for me is a plus, no one likes for a story to drag on without revelations being made.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436928i/883405.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mj019bGtIl1rnqt9wo1_500_zpse02407f7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Will you fall for Beau? YES.<br><br>Will you fall for Asher? YES.<br><br>Will your heart be crushed? Without a doubt.<br><br>How does one choose? Is the choice even up to her?<br></b><br><br><b>My Thoughts</b><br>When It Rains completely took me by surprise! Lately I felt as though I was stuck reading books that I liked but nothing about the characters left a mark and none of the story lines enraptured me the way this book did. Thus the 4.5 STAR rating! I enjoyed the writing, I enjoyed the characters and I absolutely fell in love with the story being shared. <br><b>Was I happy with the ending? YES.</b><br>The romance is sweet, extremely beautiful and steamy.*wiggles eyebrows* I highly recommend you read you read When it Rains!<br><br><b>My Ratings</b><br>Characters- Loveable, Beautiful and very sweet<br>Writing Style- Good<br>Plot/Storyline- A broken girl who finds love in two <br>Overall- I LOVED IT!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10894938497073014916" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_728133055" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728133055" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728133055?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728133055" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6068481741795236435"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437850i/885230._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br/><br/><b>This is a 2-part review with 2-separate ratings depending on whether or not you are a fan of love triangles.</b><br/><br/><b>Overall, <i>When It Rains</i>  is a well-written, highly emotional story about love, loss and healing. It's gut-wrenchingly sad at times but also has many beautiful moments and is the kind of story that really make you <em>feel</em>. </b><br/><br/>But... this is going to be a very unconventional review...  (this kind of review is always so scary for me to write but honesty always comes first</span>
  <span id="freeText6068481741795236435" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380437850i/885230._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>** FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED **<br><br><b>This is a 2-part review with 2-separate ratings depending on whether or not you are a fan of love triangles.</b><br><br><b>Overall, <i>When It Rains</i>  is a well-written, highly emotional story about love, loss and healing. It's gut-wrenchingly sad at times but also has many beautiful moments and is the kind of story that really make you <em>feel</em>. </b><br><br>But... this is going to be a very unconventional review...  (this kind of review is always so scary for me to write but honesty always comes first with me even if I run and hide in a corner after posting it)<br><br>I feel very torn about this book and, to be honest, I actually <i>wouldn't</i> have read it of my own accord had I known the details of the plot in advance because, in my eyes, this is a love triangle romance and personally, I'm just not usually a fan of them. There are certain exceptions to the rule for me but they are rare and the majority of them just don't appeal to me. In the interest of being fully open though, I'll say that different readers have varied outlooks as to whether or not this book counts as a love triangle though and the person who recommended it to me did not see it as one. I respect their opinion but simply feel differently about it.<br><br>For the record, my definition of a love triangle is when two people are in love with the same person but only one of them can be picked. In the case of this book, there were two guys in love with the same girl and she had to choose between them. It was an unconventional triangle but it still was one to me.<br><br>The specific part that bothered me here though was the heroine's decisions throughout the book regarding the two guys and so personally I will say that this book was <u>not for me</u>.<br><br>However, I realize that a) many of you <em>are</em> fans of love triangles, b) some of you might not see it as one, and c) that those of you who don't like triangles should know what this is about in order to help make a decision about whether or not you wish to read it....<br><br>So, in an effort to be fair to everyone, I have written a 2-part review. The first part will be for readers who do not usually enjoy love triangles, and the second part will be for readers who do. Each part will have a separate rating because regardless of my own personal feelings, I feel I owe it to the book to look at it objectively.<br><br><br>But before anything, here's a little about the book...<br><br>The basic story line follows the heroine, Kate, who has grown up living next door to a guy, Beau. They've been inseparable best friends and as they got older, they both knew in their hearts that they were each other's forever. Unfortunately, one rainy night without Beau there to protect her, a guy rips away a part of Kate's life, taking something from her that she could never get back.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"My once picture perfect view of the world was gone, and all that remained were a bunch of broken pieces that I couldn't glue back together."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Ashamed and confused, she kept her nightmare hidden from everyone in her life for over 2 years not even telling Beau despite how desperately he cared for her and tried to get her to open up to him about it. He knew something was wrong but he didn't know what and he was willing to wait for her, be there for her and support her no matter what.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I love you. I think I've loved you since I was five.... If you ask me to stay, I'll stay," he says, searching my eyes. I'm always worried that he'll find the truth buried in there somewhere, but he hasn't yet. I pray he never will.</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But Kate didn't feel worthy of his love and kept pushing him further and further away... and finally when he left for college, she severed nearly all their ties wanting him to go on and find his happiness without her.<br><br>At this point in her life, Asher walks in. Gorgeous, mysterious and totally into her, he pushes her to face her fears and get back the pieces of her life that were stolen from her. For whatever reason, <em>he</em> is the one she can accept help from and she falls hard for him. But he is hiding a huge secret... one that that quite literally changes <em>everything...</em> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[... and that he doesn't reveal until it's too late. Faced with the tragic outcome of his secret, Kate turns back for support to the one person who has been there all along for her and never stopped loving her, Beau.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Ok, so here goes...<br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>** PART #1 **<br><br><u>FOR READERS WHO DO *NOT* LIKE LOVE TRIANGLES</u></b>
</blockquote><br>Rating: 2.5 stars<br><br>First, if you are a fan of triangles or if the idea of the story I mentioned above doesn't bother you at all, just skip straight down to Part #2 because chances are high that you'll actually <em>love</em> this book.<br><br>I'm not going to lie though, when I first finished the book, I was pretty furious. It was beautifully written but, as a reader who desperately seeks commitment and a stable, solid relationship between characters, I found this to be a very hard read.<br><br>I think the problem was how strongly I connected with Beau in the beginning and how much I believed in their future and as such, I was honestly just incredibly frustrated with Kate. I mean I <em>tried</em> to be understanding of her given the horrible trauma she'd suffered but, at the same time, her decisions just did not sit right with me. I hated the way she kept pushing Beau away -- it hurt <em>so</em> much -- and I tried not to be judgmental because everyone copes with pain differently but it still <em>broke. my. fucking. heart.</em><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I don't know why I keep him at arm's length when it's obvious he just wants to be there for me, but I also don't know why he lets me. He just wants what's best for me, but I hate that he keeps sacrificing his own happiness to give it to me. I don't deserve it."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>I felt absolutely <em>terrible</em> for Beau and the whole situation really just made me sad because here he was desperately in love with this girl who wouldn't tell him what was hurting her and kept pushing him away. He wanted to help her so badly but she wouldn't let him. I kept trying to think of the story from his perspective and thinking of that just made my heart bleed.<br><br>See, I'd have understood it if Kate hadn't been able to let <em>anyone</em> in (relationship-wise) but she pretty much just let Asher in instantly. And I won't deny that what Asher did for her <em>was</em> beautiful - he healed her inside and out and if I hadn't been feeling so broken-hearted over Beau, I would have enjoyed the Asher parts of the story SO much more. He was a gorgeous character with a huge heart and what he helped Kate get back was admittedly priceless.<br><br>I just felt so indredibly conflicted because on one hand I loved Asher and what he was doing for Kate, but on the other hand, the price (breaking Beau's heart) was just too great for me to as fully be invested in it as I would have wanted to be.<br><br>There are readers who did not see this as a love triangle though because technically Kate wasn't in a relationship with Beau at the time that she started being serious with Asher. But I guess for me, that was just a technicality. I actually felt like she actually <em>was </em>in love with Beau from the start but, because of her trauma, she didn't feel worthy of him and couldn't admit it to herself. She'd wanted what was best for him but given how she didn't feel worthy of him, it basically felt to me like she was pushing him away for his own good, but <em>not </em>because she didn't love him... add in the fact that Beau was certainly in love with her while she was letting Asher into her life and all of this for me turned into the kind of love triangle that I didn't enjoy.<br><br>Also, like I mentioned above, there was a huge twist with Asher which I honestly guessed even before starting the book. By looking at the book cover and reading the one quote that was posted everywhere in association to the book → <em>"When it rains... Think of me." ← </em>I put two and two together.<br><br>While most of my frustration lay with Kate, Asher also did something that rubbed me the wrong way in that when he saw (in person) just how deeply Beau loved Kate, he had an opportunity to come clean about his secret and he didn't. At that point, I really felt like he should have been open about it. It was his chance and he didn't take it.<br><br>I couldn't stop thinking about how Beau must have been feeling throughout this all and it just broke my heart. I'm hiding the rest of this paragraph as a <u>SPOILER</u> because it reveals Asher's secret AND who Kate ends up with.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ It also didn't sit right with me that Kate ended up with Beau in the end (even though I know that that was what made him happy) because by that point, it felt like he was her second choice and that really she just defaulted back to him. There's this scene, right after Asher's death, where she saw Beau and... (here is a quote)... <em>"I need Beau. If I ever thought I didn't, I was kidding myself. He's been there for me from the beginning."</em> <em>←</em> I'm sorry, but that just did <em>not </em>sit right with me... it was like <i>now </i>she saw that in him?? NOW? *sigh*<br><br>It also bothered me that if Asher had still been alive, Kate would have still been with him and would never have chosen Beau. And as much as I wanted Beau to be happy, I almost wished that he had gone on to be with someone else because he didn't deserve to be anyone's second choice. But... the heart wants what the heart wants and his heart had <em>always</em> wanted Kate. She was his forever girl and he was willing to be with her no matter what.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>*sigh. I cared <em>deeply</em> for both Beau and Asher in their own way. I guess I just really really wish they were not in the same story :(<br><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>** PART #2 **<br><br><u>FOR FANS OF LOVE TRIANGLES</u></b>
</blockquote><br>Rating: 4.5+ stars<br><br>I truly believe that if you are okay with love triangles, is a good chance you may absolutely <em>love </em>this book so I'm going to try and write this as fairly as I can because if the story line doesn't bother you, then really this is a beautiful, heart wrenching and very well-written read.<br><br>The flip side to everything I wrote above is that people are not perfect. <i>Nobody</i> is. And everyone reacts to trauma differently. When something that life changing occurs, it hard to judge how it affects people so in that respect, I tried to be more understanding of Kate (and Asher to a certain extent).<br><br>Regarding the story's presentation, I have to say that I loved this author's writing style. She conveyed the emotions so vividly and was able to make me connect me very strongly to these characters right from the beginning. I'm always very impressed with a book that's able to have me nearly in tears in the first 10% because that just goes to show just how quickly I became totally <em>invested</em> in the story.<br><br>The whole book had a constant deliciously angsty feeling. It was thrilling, a little mysterious and very beautiful in many respects. It also absolutely broke my heart and made me <em>ache</em> when the twist played out.<br><br>As much as it made me sad to see how much Kate pushed Beau away, I have to admit that what Asher gave her was truly beautiful. He was insistent, pushed his way into her life and pulled her out of her shell.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I want to know you. I want to know what it is that made you cry, but more than that, I want to know what I have to do to make you happy again," he says, his voice soft.</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>He healed her, help her find herself again and brought her back to life. He gave her a second chance, he really did... I just wish he didn't have to break someone else's heart to do it.<br><br>The ending is bittersweet but as I said people aren't perfect and life certainly isn't a fairy tale. Sometimes it throws curve balls that change everything you'd planned, and sometimes it hands you a lifeline that helps you survive. Overall, the writing is beautiful, and the story is very well put together and truly made me <i>feel</i><br><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b> ** <u>CONCLUSION</u> ** </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Even though this story may not have been for me, in all honesty I do believe that many people will <strong><em>love</em> </strong>this book. It really puts your heart right through the ringer and I can see it ending up on many readers' favorites list for sure. My intention here is really <em>not</em> to deter you from reading this book.<br><br>Had I had a more accurate understanding of the direction of the story line <em>before</em> reading the book, I would<i> </i>simply <em>not </em>have read it because this is not the type of story line that appeals to me personally. That does <em>not </em>mean there is anything wrong with it. Every person reads a different book and no two people's reading experience is the same. I encourage you to check this book out and see for yourself because who knows, you may end up absolutely <em>loving</em> it.<br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_721567923" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/721567923" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/721567923?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=arcs">arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=cry-baby-books">cry-baby-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer721567923" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1322254799375512691"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436914i/883367._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='470' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I had no idea what was in store for me when Lisa De Jong offered me the opportunity to ARC this story. It’s nothing like her <i>Hearts Series</i>, this is an entirely different type of story which was for me completely <b>unforgettable</b>.<br/><br/>Please be warned…This story was <b>heartbreaking</b>. and I’m talking purchasing a full box of tissues and taking breather breaks during your read heartbreaking.<br/><br/>This is a standalone story which is told mostly in Kate the main character’s pov but we are treated to a chapter from bo</span>
  <span id="freeText1322254799375512691" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436914i/883367._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="470" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I had no idea what was in store for me when Lisa De Jong offered me the opportunity to ARC this story. It’s nothing like her <i>Hearts Series</i>, this is an entirely different type of story which was for me completely <b>unforgettable</b>.<br><br>Please be warned…This story was <b>heartbreaking</b>. and I’m talking purchasing a full box of tissues and taking breather breaks during your read heartbreaking.<br><br>This is a standalone story which is told mostly in Kate the main character’s pov but we are treated to a chapter from both of the fantastic guys, Beau and Asher. <br><br>The story starts off with your typical broken girl who’s barely living. We learn her secret that she has kept to herself for two years. Sadly, Kate has pulled out of her own life and is preparing to say goodbye to her best friend/dream boy, Beau, who is leaving for college. Kate has decided to stay home and work at the local diner, since her fear keeps her immobile.<br><br><b>
  <i>”The old Kate is gone…and she’s never coming back.”</i>
</b><br><br>Before heading for college, Beau lays his heart out for Kate who is completely shocked.<br><br><b>
  <i>”My future was taken from me, and I can’t take his too.”</i>
</b><br><br>Deciding to opt out of her future takes a toll on Kate. Until the day a gorgeous mysterious guy, Asher walks into the dinner and steals her heart and mine too.<br><br><b>
  <i>”He makes me look forward to my tomorrows, and he’s always pushing me to try new things.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kate and Asher are just <b>BEAUTIFUL</b> together. I mean beautiful as in the reason I read romance novels kind of beautiful! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436914i/883368._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Asher and Kate both have secrets but with more time they spend together they quickly learn to trust each other enough with their secrets and their hearts. <br><br>Kate slowly takes her life back with Asher helping her every step of the way. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You don’t live because of me. You live because you let me love you. You made the choice to breathe all on your own…I just helped you find the strength to inhale.”</i>
</b><br><br>Beau’s love also never lessens while Kate deals with all of Asher’s secrets.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Beau is one of the nicest people I’ve ever known, but it’s easier for me to let Asher in. Asher tries to understand me layer by layer while Beau goes straight to the center.”</i>
</b><br><br>To say certain parts of this story are sad, would be a major understatement. Especially when the events take a devastating course, I had the ugly cry going on.<br><br><b>
  <i>”I’d give anything to have forever with her. <br>Her forever…not mine.”</i>
</b><br><br>This one quote has left me thinking that is it possible for people to be lucky enough to have <b>a soul mate</b> and a <b>true love</b>. I guess some can find it in one person while others can find it in two different people...<br><br><b>
  <i>”I also realized that there’s a difference between soul mates and true love.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Is one type of love better than the other? I don’t know, but I’m lucky enough to have found them both.”</i>
</b><br><br>This story does end with an HEA so have no fear there is a light at end of the tunnel. Kate learns to love and live again. Although this story is terribly sad at times, the happy more than outshinned the tears and I just loved it! <br><br><b>
  <i>”I’ll never regret you.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>*ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.*</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1322254799375512691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s">books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=cried-big-fat-ugly-tears">cried-big-fat-ugly-tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=pure-perfection">pure-perfection</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer674547428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11382294370595400579">FIVE+++++++ Stars!!!<br/><br/>I'm going to need a moment to get over the heartache.<br/>Review to come....<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zpsb890bb71.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742393i/3118023._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zpsb890bb71.jpg' width='325' height='350' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I first would like to thank my beautiful friend, Jennifer Kyle, for recommending this book to me!!!<br/>You ROCK girl!!! ❤️❤️❤️<br/><br/>I have never, till this book, cried so hard that I couldn't breathe.<br/>I stayed up till 3am this morning to finish it.<br/>My eyes are two swollen puff bags.<br/><br/>This book "Floored" me from the Prologue!<br/>I LOVED the heroine, Kate Alexander, and that doesn't happen a lot for me.<br/>She's a beautiful 1</span>
  <span id="freeText11382294370595400579" style="display:none">FIVE+++++++ Stars!!!<br><br>I'm going to need a moment to get over the heartache.<br>Review to come....<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zpsb890bb71.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742393i/3118023._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsb890bb71.jpg" width="325" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I first would like to thank my beautiful friend, Jennifer Kyle, for recommending this book to me!!!<br>You ROCK girl!!! ❤️❤️❤️<br><br>I have never, till this book, cried so hard that I couldn't breathe.<br>I stayed up till 3am this morning to finish it.<br>My eyes are two swollen puff bags.<br><br>This book "Floored" me from the Prologue!<br>I LOVED the heroine, Kate Alexander, and that doesn't happen a lot for me.<br>She's a beautiful 19 year old girl, who had something horrible happen to her two years ago on a cold &amp; rainy night, and it's left her a broken empty shell of the girl she once was.<br>She can't stop the panic attacks that take over whenever it rains.<br>You'll learn right from the start what happened. So horrible!!!<br><br><b>I believe that life is a series of coincidences, and that night, coincidence screwed me over.</b> - Kate<br><br>She spends most of her time working in the Diner or in her room, staring at the ceiling.<br>The one bright spot in her life is the beautiful boy next door, Beau Bennett.<br>He's been her best friend since they were 5, and she's always been in love with him.<br>What happened to her, keeps her from sharing her feelings with him and even when he finally admits how he feels, she is unable to accept it because she thinks she is no longer good enough for Beau.<br>She pushes him away, when he goes off to college, thinking he deserves happiness that she'll never be able to give him.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Yes Kate, I'm going to miss you. I'm so damn in love with you, I can barely stand to spend a few hours apart from you, and now we're going to be miles and hours apart. It sucks. It really fucking sucks."</b>
</i> - Beau<br><br>I loved Beau.<br>He was so beautiful and it hurt when Kate pushed him away but we knew it wasn't because she didn't love him, it was because she loved him that she thought she was doing what was best for him.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/28dcb016c066131e2e366fbd0a81806d_zps5fde1226.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413080541i/11463657._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 28dcb016c066131e2e366fbd0a81806d_zps5fde1226.jpg" width="335" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>So Kate feels completely alone now that her one best friend is off at college.<br>Then one day, Asher comes barreling into her life.<br>There's an instant attraction &amp; connection there.<br>At first I was feeling bad for Beau but you have to remember, he was not in a relationship with Kate at that point.<br>In my opinion, this story is in no way at all a "love triangle".<br>There was never any cheating involved.<br>Each relationship was extremely necessary.<br>It helps to deliver the HEA at the end.<br><br>I felt like Asher Hunt, was brought into Kate's life, to help her heal, to make her see she was never at fault for what happened, and that she deserved so much more out of life. She needed to experience the love of her true "soul mate".<br>But Kate was also brought into Asher's life, to help him realize that he too was not at fault for the thing that happened in his past and also she was destined to be his ONE GREAT LOVE!!<br>Oh my god....I'm going to cry again!!!!!!!<br>I LOVED Asher so damn much. This man was beautiful!!<br>He's the epitome of a FANTASTIC "book boyfriend"!!!!!<br>I think most of my highlights are his words in this book.<br><br><i>
  <b>"My fact for the day:I wanted to come over here as soon as you drove away yesterday. I want to know you. I want to know what it is that made you cry, but more than that, I want to know what I have to do to make you happy again,"</b>
</i> - Asher<br><br>Kate is falling for Asher.<br>It's something she can't help.<br>He is helping her day by day to start living her life again.<br><br><b>He keeps giving me these lasting memories that make me aware of the heartbeat that still exists within me. I haven't had those feelings in so long, and I'm not sure what to do with them.</b> - Kate<br><br>They start off as friends but soon Kate and Asher are unable to deny their feelings and Kate being the beautiful person she is, does worry about Beau. She never wants her actions to hurt him because she does still love him.<br><br><i>
  <b>"I can't make promises, Kate. I want to get to know you, and I want to be there for you, but I don't think being your friend is going to work for me anymore. I want to kiss you whenever I want. I want to hold you. I want you to tell me all of your secrets and eventually tell you all of mine. I want you in my life."</b>
</i> - Asher<br><br>Asher and Kate are so deeply connected.<br>Each wants to help the other heal from their past.<br>They both refuse to tell each other their darkest secrets.<br>But one rainy night changes that.<br>He replaces a horrible memory with a beautiful one that night.<br><br><i>
  <b>"When it rains, Kate. Remember me."</b>
</i> - Asher<br><br>You'll learn Asher had one more secret he refused to share with Kate.<br>This secret was completely freaking SOUL CRUSHING!!!<br>From this point, I'm crying non stop.<br>I'm crying hard, ugly tears, that left me so stuffed up and my dog is looking at me like I'm nuts!!! <br>Just when I think I can stop crying, BAM, the author writes another gut wrenching scene.<br>I almost couldn't take it.<br>It was like having my soul tortured!!<br><br><i>
  <b>"You don't live because of me. You live because you let me love you. You made the choice to breathe all on your own...I just helped you find the strength to inhale."</b>
</i> - Asher<br><br>I hated what happened but I know it was necessary.<br><br>I have to give an honorable mention to one of the secondary characters, Ms Carter.<br>I ended up loving her!!! You think she's a minor character but in the end she was extremely important and I think gave Kate that final push she needed. I loved the napkins!!<br>Reminded me of "Effortless" and "Point of Retreat"<br><br>I did love the ending.<br>Kate deserved more than anyone to have had the chance to have that one soul mate &amp; one true love.<br><br>I think this book was beyond phenomenal and every time it even crosses my mind, I will cry.<br>I've added Asher to the top favorite book boyfriend list where he belongs!!!<br><br>Do yourselves a favor and read this one but make sure you have a box of tissues and a reading buddy for support ☺️<br><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11382294370595400579" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/595644499" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/595644499?book_show_action=true">Apr 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=weepy">weepy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer595644499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10499679986395932716"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br/><br/>I'm giving this book four stars because I feel the execution deserves it. The storyline itself did not grip me as I'd hoped, but that's due to my own personal preferences, and not the quality of the writing. <br/><br/>There were certain aspects of the plot that didn't sit well with me, namely the ending. And not for the obvious reason, but <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ I felt the guy Kate ended up with was more of a process of elimination rather than an endearing case of true love.  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/>There is a</span>
  <span id="freeText10499679986395932716" style="display:none"><b>*3.5 Stars*</b><br><br>I'm giving this book four stars because I feel the execution deserves it. The storyline itself did not grip me as I'd hoped, but that's due to my own personal preferences, and not the quality of the writing. <br><br>There were certain aspects of the plot that didn't sit well with me, namely the ending. And not for the obvious reason, but <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I felt the guy Kate ended up with was more of a process of elimination rather than an endearing case of true love.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>There is also some debate over whether or not this story embodies a love triangle, and I guess it boils down to opinion and how you look at it. I personally considered this a love triangle because of the intense emotional connection that was presented between heroine and both heroes, although it was not a deceitful one. <br><br>Yes, there are two guys deeply in love with the Kate, but she does NOT cheat nor does she switch back and forth between the two. It also helps that the three of them don't spend time together, as one guy is away at college. The way the triangle unfolds is subtle, and more about Kate finding herself after a suffering a severe trauma; it doesn't display the typical 'heroine forever drowning in her indecision' scenario. <br><br>Although I wasn't entirely invested in this story, it was heartbreaking and there were moments that touched me deeply. The beginning was insanely compelling: opening in the midst of an intense, defining moment. I do feel the intro promised more than the plot ultimately delivered, but I was still very much impressed by the power of this story. <br><br>I highly recommend this book to readers who enjoy emotional tearjerkers, and those who are not entirely opposed to love triangles of any kind. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> New Adult Romance<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Very steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> A non-deceitful love triangle.<br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Well fleshed out and equally lovable<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Heroine tries to find herself after suffers a sever trauma.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Engaging, descriptive, and gripping. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None/Standalone<br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Bittersweet at first, but then happy. Uplifting ending.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1212888154" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1212888154" />
    <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader"><img alt="Aj the Ravenous Reader" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557800982p2/30248594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1212888154?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aj the Ravenous Reader" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aj the Ravenous Reader" href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=definitely-not-young-adult">definitely-not-young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=somebody-s-sick">somebody-s-sick</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader?shelf=reality-bites">reality-bites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1212888154" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7915035450000729593"><br/><b> <i> “I think that’s the key to living a fulfilled life, having a reason or a purpose.” </i></b> <br/> <br/>Why do the most beautiful stories have to be so sad???<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426656163ra/14075171.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>This book thought my heart was some clothing item to wash, to soak in soap and water then to wring it so hard and hang it raw to dry.<br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426656163ra/14075172.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/>I’m usually always confident whenever I pick up any NA novel because I know it’s something I can easily handle emotion-wise and story-wise. But this novel is extra superlatively ultimate in exception and I wasn’t prepared </span>
  <span id="freeText7915035450000729593" style="display:none"><br><b> <i> “I think that’s the key to living a fulfilled life, having a reason or a purpose.” </i></b> <br> <br>Why do the most beautiful stories have to be so sad???<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426656163ra/14075171.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>This book thought my heart was some clothing item to wash, to soak in soap and water then to wring it so hard and hang it raw to dry.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426656163ra/14075172.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>I’m usually always confident whenever I pick up any NA novel because I know it’s something I can easily handle emotion-wise and story-wise. But this novel is extra superlatively ultimate in exception and I wasn’t prepared at all at the onslaught of the majestic tidal waves of the plot. I took a very long bath under a rain of pure heartache and pain but it was all worth it because at the end of the story, I was reminded of so many wondrous and inspirational life lessons that from now on I will never neglect.<br> <br>There are just so many things to learn in this book. It’s basically a practical guide on how to live your life despite the most bitter or painful experience you may have experienced.<br> <br><b> <i> “I realize the key to living is getting past the things I can’t change and putting my energy into the things I can.” </i></b> <br> <br>It’s also a story laying out to us the truth about true love and its difference with the concept of soulmates. It talks about finding peace and salvation in a stranger. It’s about a story of how someone could cause you so much pain but be the same person to make you whole again.<br> <br>To deliver these incredible philosophical truths, the author used a complicated but certainly well developed web of unforgettable stories and characters that will nestle in your heart and engulf your emotions. These devastatingly beautiful emotions also keep overflowing from the heartfelt words and language the writer used. I was even more pulled by the references to songs and artists I adore: “Everything” by Lifehouse, The Calling, Joshua Radin and Jeff Buckley’s “Hallelujah” (this song always puts me in this mode):<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381111621ra/4239765.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>This book also stores one of the most beautiful, non-annoying and non-cliche-ish love triangles I have read. Finally, fear not. The story ends in a beautifully inspirational and unforgettable note that will console and mend your broken heart.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7915035450000729593" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_705620727" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/705620727" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/705620727?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6852653-patrycja?shelf=2013">2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer705620727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7052274751138197422"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434618i/877455._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There is something magical and absolutely beautiful in books that can manipulate your emotions as well as change your heart. When every page is not only a part of the written story, but somewhere along, it’s starting to become a part of your reality. There is no better part of reading great story than being so tangled with it, that you ache, you cry and you’re happy for the fictional characters.<br/><br/>When It Rains has this amazing asset. It captivated me quickly with brutal honesty, raw ad gritty begi</span>
  <span id="freeText7052274751138197422" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434618i/877455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is something magical and absolutely beautiful in books that can manipulate your emotions as well as change your heart. When every page is not only a part of the written story, but somewhere along, it’s starting to become a part of your reality. There is no better part of reading great story than being so tangled with it, that you ache, you cry and you’re happy for the fictional characters.<br><br>When It Rains has this amazing asset. It captivated me quickly with brutal honesty, raw ad gritty beginning and hidden message. I was not expecting that I will be flooded with so many emotions nor did I know When It Rains will play on the strings of my soul. <br><br>When It Rains is Kate’s story, a nineteen year old, who lost her life two years ago and is now fighting to survive and forget about the night that crushed her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>
      <u>One night, one moment, one decision can<br>change the whole path that our future takes. </u>
    </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>No one knows about her secret, so Kate has to carry the weight of it on her arms by herself. She wasn’t able to tell her mother or best friend Beau. Now is time for him to go to college and leave Kate’s side and she feels entirely alone. When they share one special moment, Kate knows she has to push Beau away. She’s not good enough for him. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>
      <u>My future was taken from me, and I can’t take his too. </u>
    </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434618i/877456._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kate meets Asher in the restaurant where she’s waitressing. Few encounters later she can’t get him out of his mind. With him, for the first time in two years she feels free and happy. But he also has secrets that are breaking him. <br><br>This beautiful kaleidoscope of painful feelings mixed with hope and love, shattered my heart. Kate’s story is one of these that are hard to stop thinking about. It’s impossible to not feel anything when this novel is filled with <i> everything </i><br><br>I loved how brave Kate was despite her brokeness. I hurt alongside with her on every road she took, with every decision and consequences. Her relationship with Asher was mesmerizing. It was beautiful to see two people that understand and heal each other. How I wish things were different for them! I cried so hard, I couldn’t stop stubborn tears that kept coming and coming. <br><br>It was wonderful to see Kate when she finally opened up to someone, she changed for the better, and her love for Asher was beautiful, but still it was brutal to read about Beau and his feelings for her that never really changed.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380434618i/877457._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I ached for all of them, and when finally I understood what is going to happen, my heart almost burst from the pain. And then my hysterics began. I cried and sobbed and I felt like there’s nothing in the world that could give me relief. I overdosed on emotions. <br><br>Don’t worry, there is still HEA, that is exceptionally beautiful. But for some reason it still left me completely drained. I have never felt so destroyed and crushed by a book. When I think there is nothing that could surprise me and show me something different, a little gems like When It Rains happen. And as much as I hate feel emotional pain and cry… the feeling after it is just hard to describe. It’s <i>Katharsis </i>. <br><br>Overall, When It Rains will capture readers and enchant them. This enaging, breathaking story is painfully good written piece, that snakes it’s way into your heart and doesn’t let go, doesn’t let you breathe and what’s more it’s changes you. <br><br>I highly recommend When It Rains for every beauty and exceptional love fan. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>
      <u>I’ll never regret you.</u>
    </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><i>* ARC, courtesy of an author, in exchange for honest review. *</i><br><br><br><i>More reviews on <a href="http://smokinhotbookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Smokin' Hot Book Blog</a> and my <a href="https://www.facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog?ref=stream&amp;hc_location=stream" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Page</a><br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7052274751138197422" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1499298739" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1499298739" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1499298739?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18802206-when-it-rains">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who need to do some ugly crying</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=tragic-heartbreaking">tragic-heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=family-friendship">family-friendship</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1499298739" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17338299857033893434"><b>Genre: </b> NA Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 1 of When It Rains series<br/><b>POV: </b> First Person - Female<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423545558i/13641856.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452416707ra/17690446.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Kate Alexander and Beau Bennett had been best friends since they were kids. They told everything to each other until one day Kate had a secret she couldn’t part with. A secret that pulled her apart from everything that was good and changed their relationship.<br/><br/>Salvation came in the form of a new guy in town. Asher Hunt breathed new life into Kate. But he came with his own secret that</span>
  <span id="freeText17338299857033893434" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> NA Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b> Standalone Book 1 of When It Rains series<br><b>POV: </b> First Person - Female<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423545558i/13641856.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452416707ra/17690446.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Kate Alexander and Beau Bennett had been best friends since they were kids. They told everything to each other until one day Kate had a secret she couldn’t part with. A secret that pulled her apart from everything that was good and changed their relationship.<br><br>Salvation came in the form of a new guy in town. Asher Hunt breathed new life into Kate. But he came with his own secret that could tear them apart. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423265644i/13602509.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wanted an ugly crying book, I certainly got one with this even though it was more on the mild side lol! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>There’s a difference between soul mates and true love. Looking at the surface, they are similar, but when I dug deep down inside, I found they were different.  Is one type of love better than the other? I don’t know but I’m lucky enough to have found them both.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I do like Kate, but throughout the book I wasn’t happy with a lot of the decisions she made. She put herself in a corner and wallowed in her own misery. I understand what she went through was hard, but it was also hard to see how she was stuck on it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>He just wants what’s best for me, but I hate that he keeps sacrificing his own happiness to give it to me. I don’t deserve it.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Beau. He was sweet, caring and highly understanding. I wanted every best thing for him because he deserved it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452424833i/17691656.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As much as I love Beau, Asher stole my heart. From the moment he was introduced, he captured my attention. I love how he made Kate opened up and how they healed each other. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>We’re two people who aren’t happy when we’re apart, but can’t seem to get things right when we’re together.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>When It Rains is a beautifully heartbreaking story of friendship and love of three young individuals who are just trying to find their feet in this world. It will make you appreciate the people around you because you’ll never know when life could turn you upside down. <br><br><b>Note 1:</b> This is not a love triangle<br><b>Note 2:</b> I love the napkins thing <br><b>Note 3:</b> My eyes are a bit dry from the moisture lost hahah!<br><br><b>Books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17833493.When_It_Rains__Rains___1_" title="When It Rains (Rains, #1) by Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1374421042s/17833493.jpg" alt="When It Rains (Rains, #1) by Lisa De Jong" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19390102.After_the_Rain__Rains___1_5_" title="After the Rain (Rains, #1.5) by Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1386832867s/19390102.jpg" alt="After the Rain (Rains, #1.5) by Lisa De Jong" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18808050.Changing_Forever__Rains___2_" title="Changing Forever (Rains, #2) by Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1399435132s/18808050.jpg" alt="Changing Forever (Rains, #2) by Lisa De Jong" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18808092.Living_with_Regret__Rains___3_" title="Living with Regret (Rains, #3) by Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
