        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1577253939" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11907574651105820991">Me before reading this book:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449062113ra/17229469.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Look at all those great reviews and high ratings. I had my tissues near, prepared to cry and all.<br/><br/>Me after reading the book:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460658175i/18771801.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>There were so many things wrong with this book. I cannot write a review without <b>spoilers</b>, so If you haven't read the book, do not continue to read.<br/><br/><br/><b>Firstly</b> I would like to say that I hate any kind of violence or abuse towards women. Whoever coward chooses to abuse or violate the helpless, has to be punished by law. <br/>It is okay to have a crush on som</span>
  <span id="freeText11907574651105820991" style="display:none">Me before reading this book:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449062113ra/17229469.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Look at all those great reviews and high ratings. I had my tissues near, prepared to cry and all.<br><br>Me after reading the book:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1460658175i/18771801.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There were so many things wrong with this book. I cannot write a review without <b>spoilers</b>, so If you haven't read the book, do not continue to read.<br><br><br><b>Firstly</b> I would like to say that I hate any kind of violence or abuse towards women. Whoever coward chooses to abuse or violate the helpless, has to be punished by law. <br>It is okay to have a crush on someone. That doesn't mean that you want to do <i>anything</i> with them. I am so sorry for what happened to Kate. No girl should suffer like that. <br><br><b>Secondly</b> I would like to say that the characters feel younger than their actual age 19-23. I've read books where 16-17 yo acted more mature than them. There were grave errors in the writing, like in the part where Asher's sister in the picture has red hair, and later she's a blonde. <br>The book had similar elements from TFIOS and P.S: Ily, so many scenes that others consider shocking, didn't really shock me. Some parts were really dragging, saying the same things again and again. I was like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462193293ra/18964369.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Furthermore</b> let me discuss the characters:<br><br><b>
  <u>Beau</u>
</b>: I really didn't feel any love in the beginning between Kate and him. They have been friends for a long time, experiencing their childhood and teenage years together. I understand their bond, the affection between them and the fact that they care about each other, but that can't be love. If Beau loved Kate, why would he always seek other girls? I don't buy the BS <i>you're too good and special for me.</i> If he loved her, he should have told her.<br>I wasn't satisfied by that ending. Beau knows he'll always come second. Kate had to choose, and she <b>didn't choose him</b>.<br><br><b>
  <i>I know I will love him(Asher) forever and always<br>.............................................................<br><br>How can I find someone better when I’ve already had the best?</i>
</b><br><br> If I were Beau, I would leave Kate on her own. And the biggest BS in the book:<br><br><b>
  <i>I also realize that there’s a difference between soul mates and true love.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422338736ra/13487696.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>WTF? So, Beau is her true love, but not her soulmate. Asher was her soulmate, but not her true love. <b>Instead of dealing with halves, why don't you find someone who can be both??</b><br><br><br><b>
  <u>Asher</u>
</b>: Before <b>
  <i>the big secret</i>
</b> I didn't even like him. So what? You see someone for a moment and decide to love them because they look sad? People don't go around smiling. <br>Why would he mess around with another girl when he said he liked you that much?<br><br><b>
  <i>She came over here, and I thought I could get lost in her . . . to forget you.</i>
</b><br><br>The same crappy excuse in every Ya. Why does the author puts the heroine in such circumstances? Asher was with Kate just the day before the other girl came over. Can't they wait a little before <b>doing anything for fun</b>??? Fuck you Asher.<br>That was before <b>
  <i>the big secret</i>
</b>. After I learned what was going on with him, I wanted to feel his drama and angst, but I didn't. I didn't feel anything for him. Maybe a little sorry. <br> <br><br><b>
  <u>Kate</u>
</b>: As I said at the beginning, I am truly sorry for what happened to her. Afterwards I found her cynical and not the sharpest tool in the shed. I couldn't like her. Couldn't connect or relate with her. Many times she's a hypocrite. I still think she should have let Beau alone at the end. He will never be enough for her. He will always be the second best. Being with him is very selfish. Win/win for her.<br><br><br>Some dialogues were so poor that <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462193293i/18964370.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Asher</u>: <b>
  <i>" I’m glad I got to be your first, but I want you to promise me that I won’t be your last.”</i>
</b><br><br><u>Me to Asher</u>: You dumbass. She's 19! Of course you won't be her last! Duhh<br><br>..............................................................<br><br><u>Kate(about Asher and his father)</u>: <b>
  <i>I want to help them mend their relationship before it’s too late, but both are too stubborn to make the first move.</i>
</b><br><br><u>Me to Asher's dad</u>: You jerk. Your son is dying. This is the wrongest time to act like an asshole.<br><br>...............................................................<br><br>When Kate cries about Asher and asks her mother why do these terrible things happen<br><br><u>What could her mother have said</u>: Life's like this <b>or</b> C'est la vie <b>or</b> Some things just happen <b>or</b> we can't take everything for granted---Something that could make Kate feel better. <br><br>What she said??<br><br><u>Kate's mother</u>: I dunno.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455654286ra/18132564.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>...............................................................................<br><br>In the last scene, Kate is kissing Beau and the rain begins to fall. As he told her, <b>Whenever it rains, you think of me</b>, she looks up and smiles and thinks about him.<br><br> <b>Kissing Beau and thinking about Asher!!!</b> ARE YOU SERIOUS??? That relationship is so DOOMED!<br><br>There were some nice things. The love scene between Asher and Kate was written beautifully. It was very sweet and cute. But that wasn't enough make me give another star to this book.<br> The next book is about her and Beau. I suspect that Kate will never let Asher go, so I won't read that. It is unfair to Beau that Kate longs for another man, even if he's dead.<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1019085014" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1019085014" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1019085014?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=damn-this-guy-is-perfect">damn-this-guy-is-perfect</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=country-romance">country-romance</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1019085014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15166010212809645915"><i>
  <b>"From now on... When it rains, think of me."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>(Buddyreading this with my sis <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4590441-beatrice' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bea</a>)<br/><br/>I NEED A HUG. Can anyone just hold me while I curl up in a ball and keep sobbing now?<br/><br/>With all honesty, I don't know what to write in this review right at this very moment. I'm speechless. And I'm emotionally drained. But in a good way! :)<br/><br/>So let me start by saying that I am so glad to have read this book! I can't believe I've neglected it for months and just let it glued on my TBR. I didn't have any idea that this</span>
  <span id="freeText15166010212809645915" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"From now on... When it rains, think of me."</b>
</i> <br /><br />(Buddyreading this with my sis <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4590441-beatrice" rel="nofollow noopener">Bea</a>)<br /><br />I NEED A HUG. Can anyone just hold me while I curl up in a ball and keep sobbing now?<br /><br />With all honesty, I don't know what to write in this review right at this very moment. I'm speechless. And I'm emotionally drained. But in a good way! :)<br /><br />So let me start by saying that I am so glad to have read this book! I can't believe I've neglected it for months and just let it glued on my TBR. I didn't have any idea that this book was this good!<br /><br />When it Rains is not just your average, flirtatious chick-lit NA Romance. It's way stronger, deeper, and more emotional than you can ever imagine. It's a story about a girl named Kate who had a very painful and traumatic experience when she was in high school. What happened to her changed her emotionally. It led her to becoming aloof and distant to the people she loved, including Beau-- her childhood best friend who was always there for her when she needed him. The story became remarkable when Asher Hunt entered into her town and into her life, eventually making her fall in love with him and daring her to face her fears and troubles. Over time he taught her a lot of things which totally changed the way she perceived about her past and her future.<br /><br />If you ask me about the book's overall impact to me, I could not express it. To tell you honestly, this book was not an easy read. It was a lot to handle and it took me a lot of strength not to cry harder... because I DID CRY. This book hurt me it cuts so deep!<br /><br />Perhaps it's the author's writing style that made me feel drawn to it. Lisa De Jong used the kinds of words (and they are even quotable ones) that really create a trail of emotional wreckage in my heart. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Love is the most powerful emotion that lives inside us all. And when you have it, it can help diminish all the painful emotions that bury themselves too deep to be seen.</b>
</i> <br /><br />*sobs*<br /><br />There are also many elements of truth in this book. Basically it taught me a lot of things. I realized at some point how not being able to control certain situations but being able to move forward after everything that happened can make a difference in your life. <br /><br />This book does not only center on a love story-- love triangle story at that, but it also tackles on violent issues. This is an intense, heavy drama book and to those of you who are planning to read this, I advice you guys to grab a big box of tissues because it really stings so bad. <br /><br />But even though this book encourages ugly tears, it is nevertheless a heart-warming one. It's well-written and downright beautiful! I love that I was able to connect myself with the characters and the plot itself without having any difficulty. The book, as a whole, has many surprises. This now belongs to my list of favorites.<br /><br />Thank you so much, Ms. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6670530.Lisa_De_Jong" title="Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">Lisa De Jong</a> for such a heartfelt, wonderful tale! <br /><br />Rating: 5 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="15166010212809645915" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1525496270" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1525496270" />
    <a title="Michelle " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23450274-michelle"><img alt="Michelle " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544751386p2/23450274.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1525496270?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle " href="/user/show/23450274-michelle">Michelle </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=surgary-sweet">surgary-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=bestfriends-to-lovers">bestfriends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23450274-michelle?shelf=pissed-me-off">pissed-me-off</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1525496270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16998338493323986778">4 stars for first half/ 3 Stars for the last half!<br/>I'm really angry with this book! I loved it and hated it. <br/><br/>So it starts off pretty heavy with something horrible happening to Kate. Something that changes her life forever. Then we skip to two years later I believe. Kate has pushed everyone out of her life except for her best friend Beau and her mom. I get that Kate didn't want to tell anyone what happened to her. I get why she pushed all her friends away and even Beau. I felt like she would maybe</span>
  <span id="freeText16998338493323986778" style="display:none">4 stars for first half/ 3 Stars for the last half!<br />I'm really angry with this book! I loved it and hated it. <br /><br />So it starts off pretty heavy with something horrible happening to Kate. Something that changes her life forever. Then we skip to two years later I believe. Kate has pushed everyone out of her life except for her best friend Beau and her mom. I get that Kate didn't want to tell anyone what happened to her. I get why she pushed all her friends away and even Beau. I felt like she would maybe start to heal after they all left for college and she didn't have to hear what's wrong with you all the time. I felt really bad for Beau. But I was also glad he went away to college. <br />So I was really loving it when in walks a total stranger and he starts bringing Kate back to life. I loved Asher. I loved how sweet he was with Kate. I loved how he left her notes on napkins from the diner she worked at. I loved the fact game they played. I loved how he did everything to make her forget about that horrible night two years ago. I knew he was hiding secrets and I knew it was not going to be pretty once the second one came out. Damn! It was sad! Sad! Sad! Sad! <br />Now to the part that pissed me off. <br />spoiler alert!<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I hated how fast Kate ran back to Beau. She wanted him there at Asher's funeral. Please!! He told you he was in love with you before he left for college and you pushed him away! Then you went and opened up to a complete stranger and fell in love with him. That made me feel sorry for Beau all over again. I'm sorry Kate and Beau together just didn't work for me any longer. I mean if Asher hadn't died I don't know if she would of even thought about Beau for very long. I wasn't feeling it. It made my rating drop.&lt;\spoiler&gt;<br />Will I be reading more in this series. I doubt it. Too sad for me! <br />If you feel the urge to be depressed this one is for you to read. lol Nothing against the writing. I loved it. It just was a very sad book and I like to read happy books I guess. Happy books that don't piss me off in the end:)) lol <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>
  <a data-text-id="16998338493323986778" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_710863632" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/710863632" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/710863632?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-hate-love-triangles">i-hate-love-triangles</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710863632" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2510685083314427811">Full review now posted. <br/><br/><u>
  <b>Initial feelings after finishing the book</b>
</u><br/>Usually when it rains, I like having an umbrella handy. After reading this? No. Nope. Scratch that. I NEED A FREAKING TARP. Cue the rain. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381275194ra/4629875.gif' width='300' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><u>
  <b>Final thoughts (after a 10-hour breather)</b>
</u><br/><br/>I am so bloody angry. Don’t get me wrong here; there are <i>definitely</i> moments where I cried (like the entire second half of the book), and scenes that nearly broke my heart, but the general consensus I got was anger. So since my feelings aren’t unifo</span>
  <span id="freeText2510685083314427811" style="display:none">Full review now posted. <br><br><u>
  <b>Initial feelings after finishing the book</b>
</u><br>Usually when it rains, I like having an umbrella handy. After reading this? No. Nope. Scratch that. I NEED A FREAKING TARP. Cue the rain. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381275194ra/4629875.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>Final thoughts (after a 10-hour breather)</b>
</u><br><br>I am so bloody angry. Don’t get me wrong here; there are <i>definitely</i> moments where I cried (like the entire second half of the book), and scenes that nearly broke my heart, but the general consensus I got was anger. So since my feelings aren’t uniform, I’m going to split this review into THREE parts based off of my emotions because they changed <b>
  <i>drastically</i>
</b> and <i>
  <b>suddenly</b>
</i> in each part. Before that, though, here’s a book outline of the main events:<br><br>Kate is only 17 when she endures a horrifyingly traumatic event (I always cringe when <i>this</i> kind of event happens) on a rainy night, without her best friend and protector Beau Bennett there to save her. <br><br><b>
  <i>“That night I retreated into darkness, where my night sky had no stars, my days had no sun, and all hope was drained from my body.”<br><br>“It was the night my life ended.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ashamed, frightened, and scarred, Kate transforms from her cheery, outgoing self into an introverted, skittish woman. She hides her secret for two years, not even relenting once to tell Beau, who is so hopelessly in love with her and is desperate to know what changed her in the last two years. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Why? Please help me understand. You shut everyone out of your life. You haven’t done much of anything in two years. It’s like one day you were happy, carefree Kate, and then the next you were gone. What happened to you? I can’t fix it if you don’t tell me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Kate, however, felt dirty, broken, and undeserving of Beau’s love, pushing him further away from her. When it was time for Beau to leave for college, she bluntly tells him to go on and find happiness in his life, and almost severs all ties with him. <br><br>So while Kate is still in her hometown, barely scraping by, Asher walks into her life. And it’s like…insta-connection. A beautiful, mysterious man, Asher seems to be the only one able to pick up Kate’s broken pieces. BUT…Asher is also hiding a painful secret. A secret that will <b>
  <i>tear</i>
</b> her apart and send her right back into the arms of Beau, the boy who never stopped loving her. <br><br><u>
  <b>Part 1 (first half): Anger</b>
</u><br><br>I think of myself as a headstrong and stubborn woman, so Kate’s character is instinctively a turnoff for me. I disliked how she always referred to Beau as her protector, and on the night of her ordeal, she thinks that Beau would’ve saved her if he was there, almost as if <i>everything</i> she does, she <i>needs</i> Beau there. Please note, I am in <b>
  <i>NO WAY</i>
</b> suggesting that what happened was her fault; in fact, that is the very <b>
  <i>LAST</i>
</b> thing I would say. I’m just pointing out how my own personality is the complete opposite of Kate’s which is why I struggled so much to understand the decisions she made.<br><br>Before I go on, I <i>need</i> to point out how emotionally provocative Lisa De Jong’s writing is, and that it is a truly heart-wrenching read. Perhaps that is the reason why I connected so strongly with Beau in the beginning, and couldn’t accept Asher’s role in Kate’s life. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Yes, Kate, I’m going to miss you. I’m so damn in love with you, I can barely stand to spend a few hours apart from you, and now we’re going to be miles and hours apart. It sucks. It really fucking sucks.”</i>
</b> -Beau<br><br>Never mind Kate, it ripped <b>
  <i>my</i>
</b> heart out to see how Beau suffered from her lack of communication and the distance she put between them. And I’m not going to lie, I found it a relief when he left for college, because he truly deserves someone better. Someone stronger than who Kate was, and someone who won't let her emotional scars dictate her life. Again, this is my personality warring against Kate’s so please don’t take this personally. <br><br>I would’ve understood and sympathized with Kate more if she couldn’t let <i>anyone</i> into her life, her secrets, but that wasn’t the case. To me, it was like she <i>
  <b>instantly</b>
</i> let Asher in without many reservations. I couldn’t help but compare his efforts to that of Beau’s and I got a bad taste in my mouth, for Beau tried <b>
  <i>so hard</i>
</b> to help her, to fix her, to <i>be there for her</i>, and I felt like Kate swiped away his efforts without a blink of her eye. Maybe if I wasn’t so heartbroken over Beau, I would’ve been more accepting of Kate and Asher. <br><br><u>
  <b>Part 2 (second half): Bitter sadness</b>
</u><br><br>While I am admittedly saddened that Kate couldn’t find to accept Beau’s efforts, I don’t deny that Asher is a plus in her life. At this point of the story, coupled with Lisa De Jong’s passionately descriptive and addictive writing style, I could find myself accepting and supporting Asher and Kate as a couple. <br><br>Here it comes. Cue the angst, frustration, bitterness, sadness, tears, and fury.<br><br>***PAUSE***<br><br>I pretty much figured out Asher’s “secret” 200 pages before it was actually revealed, and on my way reading there, I was just praying and hoping it wasn’t the case. All I can say here without being spoilery is to commend Ms. De Jong for breaking my heart even further. Actually, you didn’t just break it. You tore it up in pieces and scattered them to the corners of Earth where I can never get them back. You forced me to accept what I deemed unacceptable, and then you tore that away from me too. All those emotions I cued before the pause? Those are what I feel towards you, Ms. De Jong. <br><br><u>
  <b>Part 3 (last few chapters): Anger, frustration</b>
</u><br><br>This is where I address the “love triangle.” To me, the whole Beau-Kate-Asher ring is <i>
  <b>NOT</b>
</i> a full love triangle, but it crosses the friendship boundaries. Why do I say it is NOT a full love triangle? While both Beau and Asher <i>deeply</i> love Kate, only one of them is <b>physically</b> there with her, while the other is located elsewhere, so to me, this story falls in between a love triangle and not-a-love-triangle. All three characters hardly have a moment together where they interact with each other.<br><br>Because of the <i>circumstances</i> (that’s putting it lightly) a certain character has, I finished this book feeling like the other boy would always be Kate’s <i>
  <b>second choice</b>
</i>. I felt if events hadn’t happened the way they did, she would have <i>
  <b>definitely</b>
</i> ended up with the other. And I didn’t like that. It would’ve been better if Ms. De Jong ended the story <i>without</i> adding in Kate getting together with the other character.<br><br><b>
  <u>Now for the rating</u>
</b>:<br><br>I <b>cannot</b> rate this book. I have way too many conflicting emotions and for me, rating a book solely on how it made me feel would be shallow. I take into consideration plot, writing style, character development, emotions, etc...so I guess a breakdown would be more accurate.<br><br>Plot: 2.5<br>Writing style: 5+<br>Character development: 4<br>Emotions: 5 (for making me really <i>feel</i>, despite most being ugly emotions)<br>Kate: 2<br>Asher: 4 (not 5 because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he died <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)<br>Beau: 5<br><br>This was me writing the review:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433967ra/873687.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="2510685083314427811" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_728930134" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728930134" />
    <a title="Kirsty" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty"><img alt="Kirsty" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1409522343p2/10389044.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728930134?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kirsty" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kirsty" href="/user/show/10389044-kirsty">Kirsty</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10389044-kirsty?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728930134" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11378132033131443390"><b>I think there is a right and a wrong way to do a love triangle.. (and dammit yes, this was a freaking triangle) unfortunately, for me, this was totally the wrong way.</b><br/><br/>Apparently I am in the minority here because everybody else on my Goodreads friends list absolutely loved this book. Don't get me wrong, I did enjoy it, but the ending pissed me off beyond belief and it made me feel like the rest of the book wasn't genuine and kind of a waste of my time. Yep, I'm mad.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I hate him.<br/>The old Kate</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText11378132033131443390" style="display:none"><b>I think there is a right and a wrong way to do a love triangle.. (and dammit yes, this was a freaking triangle) unfortunately, for me, this was totally the wrong way.</b><br><br>Apparently I am in the minority here because everybody else on my Goodreads friends list absolutely loved this book. Don't get me wrong, I did enjoy it, but the ending pissed me off beyond belief and it made me feel like the rest of the book wasn't genuine and kind of a waste of my time. Yep, I'm mad.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I hate him.<br>The old Kate is gone... and she's never coming back.<br>And I'll always hate when it rains."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Gah.. this book suckerpunched me right in the beginning. The prologue starts off and it's.. brutal. Many authors hint to something awful like <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[rape <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> happening to a book character, but very few actually go in to the details. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6670530.Lisa_De_Jong" title="Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">Lisa De Jong</a> didn't hold back here, every raw, gritty and painful detail was there for the reader to appreciate and really get in to Kate's head. I felt for her straight away. So the fact I hate which turn things took in the end has no bearing on what happened to Kate, it's just a crappy way she dealt with things.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I have lots of moments I'd like to hold on to forever, but I'm afraid they will always be overshadowed by that one horrible memory I can't let go of."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Kate has a best friend, Beau, who has been there for her every single day for the last two years. Since she has been dealing with the aftermath of <i>that</i> horrific night. Kate doesn't realise it, but Beau is really holding back on his feelings. He sees Kate as so much more than just a friend, but knowing she doesn't return his feelings he just plods along. Until he leaves for college and lays it all out on the table.. yep, that didn't go well. To be honest, I didn't dislike Beau, but I didn't like him either. <b>I had no feeling whatsoever.</b> I am sure that wasn't the authors intent, but because he wasn't actually present for a large chunk of the book, I found it way too hard to actually feel anything towards his character. I didn't know him.<br><br>And in comes Asher... I loved Asher <b>instantly.</b> There was just something about him and I knew from the off that he was going to be <b>my</b> choice. He was mysterious, hiding his own demons, but the feelings he had for Kate just shined through the pages. He was sweet, caring and had such a way with words. <b>
  <i>"I'd love to see you smile once in a while."</i>
</b> I just enjoyed every single thing about his character. He didn't push Kate, he didn't force her to face something she wasn't ready for, he was patient and perfectly understanding. All throughout the book he was the perfect choice for Kate, in my eyes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382180044ra/5737408.gif" width="400" height="343" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>So why did I have such a problem with the book, especially the ending? I'm afraid I'm going to have to put this in a spoiler tag because there's no way I can share my feelings without spoiling the book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[SHE EFFIN KILLED ASHER OFF. WHERE THE FREAKING HELL DID THAT COME FROM? Maybe I should have got the hint with the tag on the book, but hell no I did not. I knew he was hiding something, a big secret, but effin cancer? NO. Ughhhhhhhh I am SO PISSED. I really <b>hate</b> when an author uses something like a DEATH to get the chick out of a love triangle. There are other ways to choose, you don't have to kill one off! Oh I am SO mad. In all honesty I think I could have accepted the ending if that big fat death hadn't happened, and Kate had had to <b>choose</b> to be with Beau. But as it was? Nuhuh I am not having that. I can even accept that Kate and Beau shared something really special, something that started way before Asher even came in to the picture, but the way she dealt with it was fucking disrespectful in my eyes. Her boyfriend, the guy who saved her from herself and the darkness that was consuming her, hadn't even been dead 5 minutes before she is allowing another guy near her, sharing that they love each other. It made me feel as though she was disregarding everything that she had with Asher. <b>I hated it</b>. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I realise if you don't want to know details of the book, it's kind of hard to understand. I just don't appreciate it when an author takes a <i>certain</i> route when trying to get to the bottom of a love triangle. Unfortunately, that's what happened here and I don't agree with it at all.<br><br>It's so hard to rate this book because I did really, really enjoy it and I devoured it in such a short time. I only do that when I am really in to a book. And the writing was incredible.. it kept me engaged and interested, but I can't rate it 5* when I hated the ending so much. 3 stars seem harsh for such great writing, but is it a 4* read when I have such strong negative feelings towards it too? I don't know. I have to ponder it for a while. But for now, I'll leave you with this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382181773i/5738675.jpg" width="400" height="533" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="11378132033131443390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12399374513132695249">No no no... I would have never started this book if I had known what it involved.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503511592ra/23669679.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I know everyone's triggers may differ. For some, it is cheating and for others, it is love-triangle. But I guess some issues like rape, pédophilie or death are bound to be mentioned about as a major trigger at all times.<br/><br/><u>Personally, I can cope with some ugly issues but please, pretty please warn me if you see me reading a book that involves one of these:</u><br/><br/>1. Cancer<br/>2. Death of one or more of the main characters<br/>3. BDSM /</span>
  <span id="freeText12399374513132695249" style="display:none">No no no... I would have never started this book if I had known what it involved.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503511592ra/23669679.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I know everyone's triggers may differ. For some, it is cheating and for others, it is love-triangle. But I guess some issues like rape, pédophilie or death are bound to be mentioned about as a major trigger at all times.<br><br><u>Personally, I can cope with some ugly issues but please, pretty please warn me if you see me reading a book that involves one of these:</u><br><br>1. Cancer<br>2. Death of one or more of the main characters<br>3. BDSM / rape fantasies / daddy fantasies / pédophilie<br><br>P.S. Not that it is a big deal but I don't like books when there is pregnancy &amp; babies before the epilogue...<br><br>**********************************************<br><br><b>Now, about this book, WHEN IT RAINS…</b><br><br>It is written with 1st person point of view for the most part of the book but towards the end, there are chapters written by 2 other characters.<br><br>In a few places, there are inconsistencies (editing mistakes).<br><br><b>There are 3 main characters in the book:</b><br><br>There is a girl, Kate &amp; there are two guys, Beau and Asher. <br><br>Kate has to endure 2 different traumatic events within 3 years of her lifetime. Not being able to deal with them properly, she is sometimes really frustrating. <br><br>Both Beau and Asher are likable heroes on the surface. But they have their own flaws that I can never forgive. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[One is clueless for 2 years about how to help his best friend and the other is too selfish and he causes her 2nd trauma. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And please tell me what kind of BS is this explanation at the end of the book? <br>WTF, really?<br><br><b>I realize that there’s a difference between soul mates and true love. Looking at the surface, they are similar, but when I dug deep down inside, I found they were different.<br>...<br>Is one type of love better than the other? I don’t know, but I’m lucky enough to have found them both.</b><br><br>Oh no, no... just no... <br>You can't make me accept this explanation and the examples you give later. <br>Just no! <br>Your soul mate is your true love. The rest is just BS!<br><br><br><b>There are 2 real villains in the story: </b><br><br>One is a guy called Drew and the other is the writer Ms. De Jong herself, who thought one major trauma wasn’t hard enough to bear for Kate and us readers and added an unexpected second major trauma to the mix. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1503511591ra/23669678.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, I will warn you about both, but please <b>DO NOT LOOK AT THE SPOILERS</b> if you are brave enough to read anything and if you don’t mind <b>very sad issues</b>. Because what I will say may spoil it all.<br><br>Normally, I try to write spoiler-free reviews as I want everyone to be surprised by good plot twists but here I cannot advise you to go blind, <b>I cannot “not warn” you. </b> I need to say it under “major spoiler alerts”...<br><br>So please proceed with caution from now on, as <b>MAJOR SPOILERS ARE COMING!!!!!</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>1.	Rape of one of the main characters<br>2.	Terminal illness (cancer) and death of one of the main characters<br>3.	The couple who end up with each other at the end of the book were not always together for the major part of the book; there was another love in-between! A very good and a major love - one which is unforgettable… <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>**********************************************<br><br>It was too hard to rate this book. Without the 2nd trauma, it would have been a 4-star read for me. But now, I regret reading this book. So now, the highest I can give is 2 stars. <br><br>Personally, I wouldn’t recommend this book because it is too sad and is full of frustrating characters. <br><br>Sometimes, as in the case of Tabitha Suzuma’s book FORBIDDEN, some books are so special and unique that they are worth suffering from the great pain they cause, but not this one…. This is unnecessary in my opinion. There is drama just for the sake of drama. If you want to ugly cry, go read FORBIDDEN. It will be worth your tears, I promise.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1125148237" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1125148237" />
    <a title="Alice" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21423168-alice"><img alt="Alice" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440440940p2/21423168.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1125148237?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alice" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alice" href="/user/show/21423168-alice">Alice</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21423168-alice?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21423168-alice?shelf=read-asap">read-asap</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1125148237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14335476677105163750">Well, I am finally ready to write a review of this book. <br/><br/><b> Who am I kidding?! </b> The truth is that I won't never be ready enough, but this story really deserves one, so, <i> keep it together, Alice! </i><br/><br/>Only three books made me cry so hard that I couldn't even breathe: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15507958.Me_Before_You' title='Me Before You by Jojo Moyes' rel='nofollow noopener'>Me Before You</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_' title='Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth' rel='nofollow noopener'>Allegiant</a> and now we have another lucky one, ladies. <b> This book. </b><br/><br/><br/><br/>Kate and Beau have been bestfriends since she moved to Carrington when she was five. <br/><br/><i> "What's your name?" he finally asks.<br/>"Kate" I say, shielding the sun from m</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14335476677105163750" style="display:none">Well, I am finally ready to write a review of this book. <br><br><b> Who am I kidding?! </b> The truth is that I won't never be ready enough, but this story really deserves one, so, <i> keep it together, Alice! </i><br><br>Only three books made me cry so hard that I couldn't even breathe: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15507958.Me_Before_You" title="Me Before You by Jojo Moyes" rel="nofollow noopener">Me Before You</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18710190.Allegiant__Divergent___3_" title="Allegiant (Divergent, #3) by Veronica Roth" rel="nofollow noopener">Allegiant</a> and now we have another lucky one, ladies. <b> This book. </b><br><br><br><br>Kate and Beau have been bestfriends since she moved to Carrington when she was five. <br><br><i> "What's your name?" he finally asks.<br>"Kate" I say, shielding the sun from my eyes. "What's yours?"<br>"Beau. Like a bow and arrow. My dad likes to hunt" he says, smiling again. </i><br><br>But at the age of seventeen, something ugly happened to Kate. She's no longer the girl she used to be.<br>From that moment, she pushes everyone away.<br>When <i> Beau leaves for college </i> two years later, she feels like <i> her world is falling apart</i>. Beau was the only person in her life who still had the power to put a smile on her face.<br><br>She didn't really expect someone like Asher , the new boy in town, to come into her life.<br><br><i> My fact for the day: I wanted to come over here as soon as you drove away yesterday. I want to know you. I want to know what it is that made you cry, but more than that, I want to know what I have to do to make you happy again." </i><br><br>That's all I will say about the plot because I don't want to spoil anything to you. You simply have to read this story. <br><br>It was an emotional roller coaster, but definitely worth it. This story made me <b> FEEL </b>.<br><br>I almost DNFed this book ( and I never dnf books), not because I wasn't enjoying it, but <b> because I was so scared, I knew I was going to cry hard for this. </b><br><br>I am so glad that I kept reading. It was just what I needed. I needed a book that could suck the life out of me, <b> a book that could rip my heart out and shred it into a million pieces. </b><br><br>I finished reading this book two days ago and my mind still goes there. Just to give you an idea of <b> how hard this book affected me. </b><br><br>I was so scared about the ending, but, on my opinion, the author did an amazing job and I can say that I was happy with it.<br><br>The writing was amazing. It was just the finishing touch to this wonderful story.<br><br>This book will teach you not to take anything or anyone for granted, to seize the day, to be grateful for what you have in your life.<br>It will teach you that there's always a way to come out of the dark, you only have to find your inner strength.<br><br><i> "You don't live because of me. You live because you let me love you. You made the choice to breathe all on your own...I just helped you find the strength to inhale." </i><br><br><br><br><blockquote> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419012221i/12966912._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote><br><br><br><i> Thanks to my buddy <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/29191994-kar-" rel="nofollow noopener">Karez</a> for joining, I would have lost it without you &lt;3 </i><br><br><i> And thanks to my dear <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/14302918-patty-belongs-to-archer-hale" rel="nofollow noopener">Patty</a> for being there for me &lt;3 </i><br><br>Okay, now I'm going to listen to some depressing songs and cry a little more..<br><br>If you have not read this, please read it. Don't be afraid, you won't regret it. <br><br><br><br><br><i> Feelings after finishing the book: </i><br><br><blockquote> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382496417ra/5925721.gif" width="300" height="280" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396229021ra/9104354.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm feeling <b>empty</b> right now..I cried non-stop for the last three hours..gosh, THIS BOOK KILLED ME..hope to find some comfort in ice cream..<br><br><blockquote> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401318569ra/9785843.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </blockquote>
<br><br>I'll write a proper review soon, I'm a mess right now and I just can't..</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16406690746536725068"><b>5 <i>"Rainy"</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps259471e6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419123751i/12992513._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps259471e6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is the most heart-breaking, tear-falling, and most beautiful story I've ever read. It's a story about finding yourself, second chances, and what does it really mean to live? <br/><br/>Kate was the girl who had her life all planed out. She was the good-girl, good-grades kinda girl. She was on the track team and she had lots of friends. But everything can change in an instant. Just like how Kate's life changed in a very rainy day. <br/><br/><b>“The old Kate is gone . . . and she’s never coming ba</b></span>
  <span id="freeText16406690746536725068" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>"Rainy"</i> Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps259471e6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419123751i/12992513._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps259471e6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is the most heart-breaking, tear-falling, and most beautiful story I've ever read. It's a story about finding yourself, second chances, and what does it really mean to live? <br><br>Kate was the girl who had her life all planed out. She was the good-girl, good-grades kinda girl. She was on the track team and she had lots of friends. But everything can change in an instant. Just like how Kate's life changed in a very rainy day. <br><br><b>“The old Kate is gone . . . and she’s never coming back.<br>And I’ll always hate when it rains”</b><br><br>Now Kate is just a living soul. She's no longer the old fun-outgoing Kate, she's now the broken-miserably-friendless Kate. The only person that stood by Kate is the amazing Beau. Beau knows that something changed his Kate and he will do everything to know what happened so he can help her and understand. <br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps6852ed14.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419123751i/12992514._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps6852ed14.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now Beau is leaving for college and this gave Kate a time to think. What will she do with Beau not being around? It gets hard for their relationship because Kate wants Beau to live better.She doesn't want him to be stuck with her forever, but obviously they miss each other. Then there's Asher. The new kid in town. Rumor has it that he's a bad boy. He made it his goal to make Kate smile. To make her feel again. They start off as "friends" then they become more. <br><br> <a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps5445e04e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419123751i/12992515._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps5445e04e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book was so beautiful. I've never read such an emotional book before. The way it's put together is amazing. It was a teary book for sure. I just have no other words to describe it anymore. This book tough me a lesson 'Never take life for granted, always live it to the fullest'. <br> I highly recommend this book to those haven't read it yet.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps48a81681.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>“You light up my world even in my darkest moments.”</b></span>

<div id="review_731282521" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/731282521" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/731282521?book_show_action=true">Sep 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer731282521" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9039402227690014799">3.5 - 4 ★'s<br/><br/>Kate's had your fairly happy childhood, growing up with her best friend, Beau, who lives next door. But everything changes one night and it's something she feels she cannot tell another soul, not even her best friend and she pushes everyone away until she is all alone. That is, until Asher shows up. <br/><br/>Wow...this is not a book for the faint of heart. This book is intense and heavy and will make you bawl like a little baby. <br/><br/>There are two very heavy events in the book, both of them equally</span>
  <span id="freeText9039402227690014799" style="display:none">3.5 - 4 ★'s<br><br>Kate's had your fairly happy childhood, growing up with her best friend, Beau, who lives next door. But everything changes one night and it's something she feels she cannot tell another soul, not even her best friend and she pushes everyone away until she is all alone. That is, until Asher shows up. <br><br>Wow...this is not a book for the faint of heart. This book is intense and heavy and will make you bawl like a little baby. <br><br>There are two very heavy events in the book, both of them equally awful. The events do not bother me but I questioned the reasoning behind the second one. One thing's for sure, it made the romances easier.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399159489i/9516523.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yes, <b>
  <u>romances</u>
</b>!! It's not really a triangle per se. Kate and Beau grew up together and eventually fell in love but before anything could come of it, event one happened. And by Kate keeping the first event a secret from Beau, she was able to get him to leave for college without her. In turn, when Asher shows up, Kate is free to be with him without <i>much</i> guilt. <br><br>It's really hard at this point because you've gotten to know Beau and <i>like</i> him. I had a hard time wanting Kate to have anything to do with Asher especially finding out he has secrets of his own. <b>But</b> Asher grows on you. He's just so sweet to Kate. <i>~ I love the napkin notes and...questions of the day, milkshakes with french fries and her necklace! ~</i> I think that makes second event even worse. It did really help to get his POV from time to time. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399158740i/9516465.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's some good steamy scenes...not very graphic but very sweet and loving. I was actually surprised at how easily things worked out. <br><br>Naturally, there's lots of drama *cue the crying* and it feels like it will <i>never end</i>!! The parts with Kate and her Mom killed me especially having a daughter myself. <br><br>But have faith, it does end well for the most part. However, it's just a really sad book and I would really recommend that you read the novella that comes after this, <i>After The Rain</i>. You will need that happy...trust me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/642482.gif" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Favorite quotes</b><br><br>♥ "I just thought you should know that you're the best first kiss I've ever had."<br><br>♥ “From now on . . .” <br><br><i>kiss</i>. <br><br>“When it rains . . .” <br><br><i>kiss</i>. <br><br>“Think of me.”<br> <br>♥ “You don’t live because of me. You live because you let me love you. You made the choice to breathe all on your own . . . I just helped you find the strength to inhale.”<br><br>♥ “You’re here with me. Always. Whenever I close my eyes, all I see is you.”<br><br>♥ "You light up my world even in my darkest moments."<br><br><br><b>*BR w/Melissa*</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398968638i/9490153._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9039402227690014799" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=death">death</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7591340-sarah-elizabeth?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1233149484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7054534234733459348">This was a NA contemporary story about a girl who had been raped.<br/><br/>I felt quite sorry for Kate in this, having to deal with being raped and feeling like you can’t tell anyone can’t be easy, and it was clear how much it had affected her.<br/><br/>The storyline in this was about Kate’s best friend Beau (who wanted to be more than her friend) leaving for college, and Kate falling in love with a new guy in town called Asher. I did find this a little strange at first though as Kate seemed to almost forget Beau, </span>
  <span id="freeText7054534234733459348" style="display:none">This was a NA contemporary story about a girl who had been raped.<br><br>I felt quite sorry for Kate in this, having to deal with being raped and feeling like you can’t tell anyone can’t be easy, and it was clear how much it had affected her.<br><br>The storyline in this was about Kate’s best friend Beau (who wanted to be more than her friend) leaving for college, and Kate falling in love with a new guy in town called Asher. I did find this a little strange at first though as Kate seemed to almost forget Beau, when previously he’d been all she’d thought about, and when Beau found out about Asher I felt really sorry for him.<br>We did then get another quite sad storyline that changed things completely though, and it seemed unfair that Kate had to deal with so much at such a young age.<br><br>The ending to this was okay, but I did have some reservations <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ as it seemed like Kate ended up with Beau out of convenience or by default, because Asher was dead, when she’d said previously that she didn’t love Beau that way.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433081147i/15047180.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6.5 out of 10</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6218070810628241770"><b> 4 Big raindrop sized stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/668401.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>“From now on . . .” kiss. “When it rains . . .” kiss. “Think of me.”</b><br/><br/>This one had me swooning, cringing, smiling and crying. This is a well written and beautifully played out story of a young woman who overcomes a life-changing event through the love of two young men. It is not a love triangle in the traditional sense, but to me there was always three in this love story-Kate, Beau and Asher. <br/><br/>Kate and Beau have been best friends forever. They went to school together, pl</span>
  <span id="freeText6218070810628241770" style="display:none"><b> 4 Big raindrop sized stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/668401.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“From now on . . .” kiss. “When it rains . . .” kiss. “Think of me.”</b><br><br>This one had me swooning, cringing, smiling and crying. This is a well written and beautifully played out story of a young woman who overcomes a life-changing event through the love of two young men. It is not a love triangle in the traditional sense, but to me there was always three in this love story-Kate, Beau and Asher. <br><br>Kate and Beau have been best friends forever. They went to school together, played together, love each other. But Kate can’t love Beau like he loves her and he does not understand and Kate can’t tell him why or how she truly feels about him, so she pushes him away. <br><br>Asher Hunt, the mystery man, is the one that has the power to bring the real Kate back. The connection between these two is so emotional and beautiful, I simply adored Asher. But, I also felt bad for Beau. I wanted Kate to heal, but I also did not want Beau to hurt. And I most certainly did not want… not going to say, you need to read for yourself. <br><br>Yes, I was stabbed in the heart, but then it healed and I will never look at a diner napkin without thinking of <b>“The guy who’s still smiling because of you…”</b><br><br><br>*Thank you, Lisa for sharing this beautifully touching story with me. I am so proud of you and feel privileged in knowing you, even though it has only been in the virtual sense ;-)<br><br></span>

    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beatrice by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/30248594-aj-the-ravenous-reader">Aj the Ravenous Reader</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1237430109" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5846326827604221289">I have to sit for minutes and think about what will I write on my review. Honestly, I'm numb. I don't know where will I start because this is one book that gives you that <i>heavy</i> feeling and will make your eyes puffy from crying. I swear I need a BIG HUG. My goodness.<br/><br/><i>When It Rains</i> is a beautiful, heart wrenching masterpiece. This review isn't enough to express all my sentiments. This isn't an ordinary new adult novel. I dare you guys to read this one and have some boxes of tissues beside you, as w</span>
  <span id="freeText5846326827604221289" style="display:none">I have to sit for minutes and think about what will I write on my review. Honestly, I'm numb. I don't know where will I start because this is one book that gives you that <i>heavy</i> feeling and will make your eyes puffy from crying. I swear I need a BIG HUG. My goodness.<br /><br /><i>When It Rains</i> is a beautiful, heart wrenching masterpiece. This review isn't enough to express all my sentiments. This isn't an ordinary new adult novel. I dare you guys to read this one and have some boxes of tissues beside you, as well as a pillow for you to embrace because it will be a <u>SOB-FEST</u>. This is probably one of the most heartbreaking books I've read for all time. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"Life's not fair. Life's often complicated, leaving us to deal with things that we shouldn't have to. Life can make you smile one day, only to leave you broken into tiny little pieces the next."</b>
</i><br /><br /><b>Kate Alexander</b> had a traumatic past and it's been haunting her for years. It destroys her physically and emotionally to the point she pushes everyone away even her long time best friend <b>Beau Bennett</b>. Until one day, <b>Asher Hunt</b> came to her life. She's intimidated by his looks, confidence and mysterious character. Being with him, she found comfort and security. He helped her to battle her own demons and found happiness with him. She thought everything will be okay, until she knew Asher's secret... <br /><br /><i>You know the moment when you're at the peak of happiness and all of a sudden it just crushed?</i> YES. This book just gave me that feeling. Such an emotional roller coaster. Aside from that, I love the writing style, the characters and the quotable lines. It's a heavy drama filled with lessons. Like, coping and moving on in life after a tragedy or most painful moment of your life. This is entirely different from the New Adult novels I've read. Definitely not cliche.<br /><br /><b>My Playlist:</b><br />- You and Me by The Lifehouse<br />- Tenerife Sea by Ed Sheeran<br />- She Will Be Loved by Maroon 5<br />- Demons by Imagine Dragons<br />- Ungodly Hour by The Fray<br />- You by The Carpenters<br />(including the ones mentioned in this book.)<br /><br />I am looking forward to read the next one. Hopefully, it will enlighten me. Thumbs up to Ms. Lisa De Jong!</span>
  <a data-text-id="5846326827604221289" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081190461?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081190461" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8214274898246606541"><b>5 Melt your breath away stars</b><br/><br/><b>I’ve put When it Rains on the back burner because it’s a love triangle read, but I was forced to read it and let me say this…<br/><br/>I’M SO GLAD I DID!!!!</b><br/><br/>The emotions this book made me feel…<br/><br/><b>Crazy, Intense, Angst, Heart-break, Happy</b><br/><br/>In one day Kate’s life is changed dramatically. Her best friend Beau doesn’t know where his fun loving best friend went, but he’s desperate to get her back. When Beau leaves for college Kate is trying to move forward with her life, but can’t leave </span>
  <span id="freeText8214274898246606541" style="display:none"><b>5 Melt your breath away stars</b><br><br><b>I’ve put When it Rains on the back burner because it’s a love triangle read, but I was forced to read it and let me say this…<br><br>I’M SO GLAD I DID!!!!</b><br><br>The emotions this book made me feel…<br><br><b>Crazy, Intense, Angst, Heart-break, Happy</b><br><br>In one day Kate’s life is changed dramatically. Her best friend Beau doesn’t know where his fun loving best friend went, but he’s desperate to get her back. When Beau leaves for college Kate is trying to move forward with her life, but can’t leave the past behind. That is until Asher comes into her small town.<br><br><b>Review</b><br><br>Yes, this is a love triangle read, but it’s one that is tolerable. I didn’t find Kate annoying or stupid. I found When it Rain very endearing and heart-warming. <br><br>Beau is the boy next door and you will love him. He’s sweet, perfect and is always there for Kate, but he’s going to college and Kate does not want to. When I first started this, I thought to myself, what is Kate doing? She has a perfect guy in her life, why is she pushing him away. But you really do understand why she does what she does. <br><br>I was nervous reading Kate’s interactions with Asher because I didn’t think I could move past Beau, but you will fall in love with Asher too. It’s cute reading Asher and Kate’s interactions because she’s so skittish and Asher is just so new and different, they make the perfect combination. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I may not be into superheroes, but if I were, Asher would be it for me. <br><br>We tend to regret our yesterdays, live in our todays and forget about our tomorrows, but I’m trying to cherish them all</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>There’s a lot that happens When it Rains, the book shifts probably twice before it ends and oh boy it’s a roller coaster, but the ride is so worth it.<br><br>It’s an emotional gripping tale about moving from past issues and falling in love. I highly recommend!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17833493.When_It_Rains__Rain___1_" title="When It Rains (Rain, #1) by Lisa De Jong" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1374421042s/17833493.jpg" alt="When It Rains (Rain, #1) by Lisa De Jong" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00FG9CI0K/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00FG9CI0K&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=HGMLCHY4AHGMSIU5" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
