<div id="review_673729131" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/673729131" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/673729131?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9816167-jessica-s-book-review?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer673729131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5988757439882877218"><b> <a href='http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read more reviews </a> | <a href='https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview' rel='nofollow noopener'>Find Me on Facebook</a> </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380744835i/3118389.png' width='344' height='490' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am in a complete and utter mess right now. I just finished reading When It Rains and wanted to rush and write my review right away because I had so much going in my head about this book. My mind & emotions are <b>ALL OVER</b> the place and that is a <b>WONDERFUL</b> thing. Be prepared for tissues, lots and lots of tissues! This story is heart-wrenching, heartbreaking, full of emotions that you won't be able to just walk away from these characters. I don't remember t</span>
  <span id="freeText5988757439882877218" style="display:none"><b> <a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Read more reviews </a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Find Me on Facebook</a> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380744835i/3118389.png" width="344" height="490" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am in a complete and utter mess right now. I just finished reading When It Rains and wanted to rush and write my review right away because I had so much going in my head about this book. My mind &amp; emotions are <b>ALL OVER</b> the place and that is a <b>WONDERFUL</b> thing. Be prepared for tissues, lots and lots of tissues! This story is heart-wrenching, heartbreaking, full of emotions that you won't be able to just walk away from these characters. I don't remember the last time I cried like this over a book since reading Slammed by Colleen Hoover.<br><br>Seriously- no joke this was me reading from about the 65% mark to the very end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744835ra/3118390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let’s start with the characters: <b>Kate, Asher, and Beau.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380744835i/3118391._SX540_.png" width="500" height="382" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, first thing first; there are a lot of things going on in the book world about whether When It Rains being a love triangle or not. To me personally, I did not find it a love triangle at all. Yes, there is one girl and two guys but there is no back and forth on whom Kate should be with, there was no cheating there were no promises being broken. The story is about a girl who is lost finding love in different times of her life by two different men who both bring something special to Kate <b>at different times</b>. Beau to me is a minor character; he isn’t even in the same city as Kate. He is an important character none the less but 80% of the story is of Kate &amp; Asher. That is my two cents on that on the matter!<br><br><b><i> “I can’t say I’m stuck between the two because my heart tells me over and over again that its Asher I want. But a person can’t have that much history with someone like Beau, and not carry them around with them.”</i>-Kate</b><br><br>Kate &amp; Beau have been best friends &amp; neighbors since they were five. They both liked each other and eventually fell in love but could never find the right time to tell one another how they feel. They remained friends. When Kate was sixteen she was raped and she changed. She stopped hanging out with her friends, she quit being the happy go-lucky 16 year-old and shut the world out; even Beau for the most part. Kate hasn’t told a soul what happened to her and feels like no one would understand or believe her.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744835ra/3118392.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Beau is about to leave for college and tells Kate his feelings for her <b>FINALLY!</b> She pushes him away even further and lives her life in the small town while Beau is away at school. This is when Kate meets Asher. He is new to town and the two form an instant bond, a connection that Kate can’t even explain. As hesitant as she is to trust someone new, she trust Asher. He opens her eyes again and helps her heal while falling in love at the same time. Their relationship is special, truly <i>special</i> and unique.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380744835i/3118393.png" width="350" height="444" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>“I can’t make promises Kate. I want to get to know you, and I want to be there for you, but I don’t think being your friend is going to work for me anymore. I want to kiss you whenever I want. I want to hold you. I want you to tell me all your secrets and eventually tell you all of mine. I want you in my life.”</i> -Asher</b><br><br><br><b><i>“Make me forget. I want to feel your hands on my skin. I want to hear your voice in my head over and over, saying words I want to remember instead of ones I want to forget. I want you to touch everything inside of me… every part of me.”</i> -Kate</b><br><br>This is when my heart broke for Beau… he has been there for Kate since they were five but their timing was just always off and Asher was able to break down Kate’s wall at the moment. She needed Asher just like she needed Beau in the past.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744835ra/3118394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The 65% mark of the book comes and this is when I completely lose it…. I mean I was in tears so big I had to stop reading because everything just became a blur with all the tears in my eyes. I was just not expecting the turn of events and it hit me hard. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/668223.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously, how much more can Kate go through?<br><br>The author did an amazing job of connecting the readers to the characters. I felt every ounce of pain all three felt at different times as I read; from the beginning to the end. I hurt for Kate, I hurt for Ben, and I hurt for Asher. I have had the pleasure of reading a few of Lisa De Jong’s work before and this is <b>BY FAR</b> my favorite. The writing was spectacular; the characters were deep, the story was emotional and just simply perfection. I laughed, I cried (okay, I cried A LOT), and I smiled. It had everything I look for in a book and then some.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744835ra/3118395.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The ending was as perfect as it could be… I loved the epilogue and seeing a little bit into the future. I really didn’t know how I wanted it to end… I loved Asher and Beau for completely different reasons and so did Kate. They were meant to be in her life at those certain times for a reason. She was able to <b>LIVE &amp; LOVE</b> through each man.<br><br>When It Rains is a book I can already tell will be a “Book Hangover” for me. I will be thinking about it for days and days. Asher will stay with me for a long time, he something special that is for sure. Every time I hear <i>‘Everything’</i> by Lifehouse or look at the nights sky I will think of Asher. We all need an Asher and a Beau in our lifetime if we are to be so lucky.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380744835ra/3118396.gif" width="300" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I give When It Rains 5 GIANT Stars!<br><br>Amazing job Lisa!!!! You told a beautiful story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/419651.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Book provided by the author in return for an honest review.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="5988757439882877218" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1240693214" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1240693214" />
    <a title="Kathe L" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25921490-kathe-l"><img alt="Kathe L" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421550107p2/25921490.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1240693214?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathe L" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathe L" href="/user/show/25921490-kathe-l">Kathe L</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25921490-kathe-l?shelf=romance-or-ya-book">romance-or-ya-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25921490-kathe-l?shelf=3-5-stars">3-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25921490-kathe-l?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25921490-kathe-l?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1240693214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17917469497244833968"><br/>3,5-4 stars? <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427683902i/14306523.gif' width='350' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><s>I hate this book.</s> <br/><s>I love this book.</s> <br/><br/>I don't know what I'm thinking right now. I'm definitely kind of numb. I can't rate this, but at the same time I can't not write this review right now. I <b>need</b> to pour my heart out because otherwise I will be awake the whole night thinking about it. <br/><br/><b>"Love is a confusing thing and sometimes it's hard to tell the difference between loving someone and being in love."</b> <br/><br/>One word for this book: <i>it is unfair.</i> In the beginning I hated it, because of all the</span>
  <span id="freeText17917469497244833968" style="display:none"><br>3,5-4 stars? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427683902i/14306523.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><s>I hate this book.</s> <br><s>I love this book.</s> <br><br>I don't know what I'm thinking right now. I'm definitely kind of numb. I can't rate this, but at the same time I can't not write this review right now. I <b>need</b> to pour my heart out because otherwise I will be awake the whole night thinking about it. <br><br><b>"Love is a confusing thing and sometimes it's hard to tell the difference between loving someone and being in love."</b> <br><br>One word for this book: <i>it is unfair.</i> In the beginning I hated it, because of all the things that were going on. And I hated some choices that Kate did. Besides, do you guys know how weird it is to have a character with the same name as you? It's written differently because my name is of German origin, but it is spoken in the same way. And I was like "damn, Kate, don't do that to pour Beau." And it was confusing as hell, because it was almost as if I was mad at myself. <br><br><s>Kathe, stop rambling.</s> Back to the book! We meet Kate and Beau, and afterwards we meet Asher. It is kind of a love triangle, but at the same time, it wasn't. I know is confusing, and trust me, this review is a hard one to make. This book is like a roller coaster of Kate's life. We meet happy Kate, Kate in love, Kate depressed, Kate smiling and Kate at the bottom. And while she's at it, she <b>definitely</b> brings you down with her. <br>Did I cry? For sure.<br>Did I want to smack her head against a tree? YES. <br>In other words, life wants Kate to hurt. The universe wants her to feel like this, but the universe has a point, one that is only discovered later on: in order for us to grow, we need happy and sad times so they can balance each other. We have to figure out who we are. And still, the universe gives us A LOT of warnings that this isn't exactly a happy book. It's more of a thoughtful book. <br><br>Of course, mad Kathe wanted to throw this book at a wall and cry until she didn't have any tears left. <b>"Why would any person write a book like this?"</b> - Mad Kathe. <br>But, when I realized the book wasn't over yet, in fact, it still had a lot of pages left, reasonable Kathe decided not to curl up in a ball and she decided to toughen up. I decided to see what the future had in storage for Kate. <br><br>And let me tell you, the end surprised me a bit. I thought it was going to be a repeat of the beginning. And that chapter right before the epilogue??? LIKE WOW. I know, I know, those of you who read this book must be looking at this review like "how could she be surprised at that end?" but I kind of was. But man, was I happy! And to use "happy" to describe any part of this book is hard. <br><br>But, even so, this book was incredible. I just don't know how to rate it because I'm facing an emotional breakdown. <s>I loved Asher</s>, but I loved Beau. I loved Beau more. Obviously, I chose the hardest guy to love the most. And because I made that decision, at the beginning I wanted to hate Asher. But guys, it is impossible. For the first time ever, the main character (Kate) came in like probably the fifth character I liked the most in this book and it didn't affect <s>much</s> the impact this book had on me. <br><br>All in all, you see what is coming in this book miles and miles away. But if you're one of those readers (cough cough me), who thinks everything is going to be okay WHEN IT IS NOT, then this book is going to hurt. Like a stab in the heart. Like being burned. But do I regret reading it? No, and I feel a bit masochistic (is that a word?). Yes, becoming a reader makes you develop masochist tendencies, for sure. Otherwise, why would I be happy I read this? But I am, and if you, amazing person who is reading this awful review, feel prepared, you should read this too. For sure. Because it is a deep emotional read who will leave you with a lot of doubts about how you are leaving your life. And it gives you strength to always look forward. All in all, it leaves a beautiful message that I won't forget for a while. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17917469497244833968" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_728759557" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728759557" />
    <a title="Johanna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10198457-johanna"><img alt="Johanna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393386564p2/10198457.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728759557?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Johanna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Johanna" href="/user/show/10198457-johanna">Johanna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728759557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4187182412801597339"><b>*~*~*4 Uniquely Beautiful Stars*~*~*<br/> <a href='http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/tumblr_mgo41t1J7K1qgawlzo1_500_zps18ea5077.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381460814ra/4906667.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_mgo41t1J7K1qgawlzo1_500_zps18ea5077.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><blockquote>I've been hurt.<br/> I've been saved.<br/> And I've been found.</blockquote></b><br/>When It Rains, is a unique extraordinary story of a young woman's journey of being victimized, broken, and finding herself. Kate is dealing with a personal secret that is debilitating her present and future. But its Kate self awareness and forgiveness that enables her to move on in her life.<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>I believe that life is a series of coincidences, and that night, coincidence screwed me over.</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><u>
  <b>But at what cost?</b>
</u></span>
  <span id="freeText4187182412801597339" style="display:none"><b>*~*~*4 Uniquely Beautiful Stars*~*~*<br> <a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/tumblr_mgo41t1J7K1qgawlzo1_500_zps18ea5077.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381460814ra/4906667.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mgo41t1J7K1qgawlzo1_500_zps18ea5077.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><blockquote>I've been hurt.<br> I've been saved.<br> And I've been found.</blockquote></b><br>When It Rains, is a unique extraordinary story of a young woman's journey of being victimized, broken, and finding herself. Kate is dealing with a personal secret that is debilitating her present and future. But its Kate self awareness and forgiveness that enables her to move on in her life.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I believe that life is a series of coincidences, and that night, coincidence screwed me over.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><u>
  <b>But at what cost?</b>
</u><br><br>Kate is a nineteen year old girl who suffered a traumatic incident two years prior. This said incident changed everything within her causing a ripple affect between her and her loved ones. Kate is just a shell of a person she was two years ago.<br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/Kristin-Kreuk-Leaning-On-Wall-4-1920x1200-32756_zps71e67b65.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381462396i/4907969._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Kristin-Kreuk-Leaning-On-Wall-4-1920x1200-32756_zps71e67b65.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>But before this traumatic incident occurred, Kate had a best friend named (Beau) who was her everything. He was not only her best friend but her neighbor, and the only man she's ever loved. Unfortunately, due to Kate's graphic traumatic event all she seems to be doing is pushing Beau away.<br><b>Beau &amp; Kate</b><br> <a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/tumblr_mdkiycZEpL1rjlv73o1_500_large1_zps5bc36b2f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381463858ra/4909518.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mdkiycZEpL1rjlv73o1_500_large1_zps5bc36b2f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Things turn for the best when Asher pops up in her life. Randomly out of the blue, Asher turns Kate's world upside down. But in the best way possible. The more time Kate &amp; Asher spend together the closer they become allowing Kate to heal in the process. Little does Kate know that Asher's main goal is to replace all her bad memories with new happy ones. <br><a href="http://s1285.photobucket.com/user/jayenot30/media/tumblr_maqdhrBEXl1qkjqiyo1_5001_zps7445176c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381463858ra/4909519.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_maqdhrBEXl1qkjqiyo1_5001_zps7445176c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>From now on..kiss.. <br> When it rains..kiss..<br> Think of me...</b>
</blockquote><br>Unbeknownst to Kate, Asher is keeping his own secrets. But its Asher's secret that will <b>devastate, crumple, and alter their lives forever</b><br>It's up to Kate to see where she goes from here.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Life's not fair. Life's often complicated, leaving us to deal with things that we shouldn't have to. Life can make you smile one day, only to leave you broken into tiny little pieces the next.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><b>How do you choose between TRUE love, and your SOUL Mate?</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Thoughts:</u>
</b> This was a slow paced unconventional love story about living your life to the fullest and never taking anything for granted. Love hard, and play hard! When It Rains is a emotional book about love, loss, and second chances. Asher's &amp; Kate's relationship was a beautiful heartfelt journey and was glad I went along for the ride.....</span>
  <a data-text-id="4187182412801597339" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('B0hKWPFH0D2fyt4RuoUHLZGI39F+hR/r8Vsm0h68fW8vr53q+pQtCUlF0QPbK3Q6RRzUN4uo46jqNz3X4i5Znw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('orEvAh/xSU4ayxB30tnjr3azi0gmZKS+Mcb7avI3zUSKVviwFCK0esxEH2Wzd5C4oieArtNJWP0qquBvDqXptA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
